<div id="page-2321">
<h3><a name="page-2321">Friday, February 23, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/8432' title='John Ward'>John Ward</a> (col)<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a>. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Colde enough that the land<span class='line-break'> </span> froze as he turned it up.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8431' title='Nellie'>Nellie</a> cut out some <span class='line-break'> </span> little suits for <a href='../subjects/8086' title='Jennie Owen'>Mrs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Fitz boy. She done the <span class='line-break'> </span> most of the cooking and <span class='line-break'> </span> dishwashing. <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr</a>. Thomson<span class='line-break'> </span> sent here for <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I let him have a little. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christine Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come. She wanted <span class='line-break'> </span> butter. I could not<span class='line-break'> </span> let her have any.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>. Mr. [Duepe?]<span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> and did not<span class='line-break'> </span> teach. I hope he won't <span class='line-break'> </span> be sick much.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2322">
<h3><a name="page-2322">Saturday, February 24, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> part of the day. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> olde <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>. Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a> for the first<span class='line-break'> </span> time in several months.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8431' title='Nellie'>Nellie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> some today. <span class='line-break'> </span> I cut some pieces<span class='line-break'> </span> for a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>. I [washed?]<span class='line-break'> </span> some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I let <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> go to <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Reynols</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. She is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Norman Booker</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben to Strait Stone<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna got the first <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a><span class='line-break'> </span> cup today. </p>

<div id="page-2323">
<h3><a name="page-2323">Sunday, February 25, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. We all<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home except<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry. He went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Sunday School and to<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Jim Powers. Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Johnsons. <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie made pies<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner. Today<span class='line-break'> </span> she bathed the <span class='line-break'> </span> children and dressed<span class='line-break'> </span> them. I milked and <span class='line-break'> </span> churned and helped<span class='line-break'> </span> about dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  </p>

<div id="page-2325">
<h3><a name="page-2325">Monday, February 26, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day. Ben plowed until<span class='line-break'> </span> he got wet.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie washed the clothes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Are on the fence now<span class='line-break'> </span> as wet as they can be.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie worked some button <span class='line-break'> </span> holes and got most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. She got a letter<span class='line-break'> </span> from Evylin saying she<span class='line-break'> </span> was sick. Nel has been<span class='line-break'> </span> about half crazie ever<span class='line-break'> </span> since.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to <span class='line-break'> </span> school. Come home wet<span class='line-break'> </span> to the skin in places.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie Gilbert and John <span class='line-break'> </span> got milk here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so anxious for<span class='line-break'> </span> good weather so I can<span class='line-break'> </span> get out where I <span class='line-break'> </span> please and take the<span class='line-break'> </span> baby with me. </p>

I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Norman <a href='../subjects/9433' title='Bookers'>Bookers</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7966' title='Mrs Booker'>Mrs Booker</a> gave me <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet potatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> as nice as I ever <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>saw</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so glad of them. </p>

Ben face is sore. <span class='line-break'> </span> He worked all morning<span class='line-break'> </span> cleaning up the land<span class='line-break'> </span> that he is going to plow.<span class='line-break'> </span> This morning Jim and John<span class='line-break'> </span> went to mauling.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the mill. The Blain <span class='line-break'> </span> girls passed here this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. Don't know <span class='line-break'> </span> where they had bin. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben bought a six pound<span class='line-break'> </span> can of beef for [?].</p>

<div id="page-2328">
<h3><a name="page-2328">Friday, March  2, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

I went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey. She was at<span class='line-break'> </span> work. Irvin and Duepney<span class='line-break'> </span> brought me home.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school. <span class='line-break'> </span> Dr. Owen let me<span class='line-break'> </span> go with him a part<span class='line-break'> </span> of the way. I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad of that much<span class='line-break'> </span> help. Every one is <span class='line-break'> </span> good to me no matter<span class='line-break'> </span> when I go. I would<span class='line-break'> </span> be so glad to go <span class='line-break'> </span> and see all of my<span class='line-break'> </span> folks but I may <span class='line-break'> </span> never see them<span class='line-break'> </span> again. I want to see <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie more than any<span class='line-break'> </span> one now.</p>

<div id="page-2330">
<h3><a name="page-2330">Monday, March  5, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

He sowed<span class='line-break'> </span> some peas, I think.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not done anything<span class='line-break'> </span> much today. Cut some <span class='line-break'> </span> cress salit. Helped the <span class='line-break'> </span> children shuck a shock <span class='line-break'> </span> of corn. Milked and churned.<span class='line-break'> </span> Set a hen.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie made a canvas<span class='line-break'> </span> for the plant bed this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and done some other sewing<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie washed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> The clothes did not dry<span class='line-break'> </span> much. <span class='line-break'> </span> Heard today that Lee had<span class='line-break'> </span> bin appointed commisioner <span class='line-break'> </span> of the I don't know what.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Booker sent and <span class='line-break'> </span> got the quilting frames<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Guess she<span class='line-break'> </span> is fixin to quilt some. </p>

<div id="page-2332">
<h3><a name="page-2332">Tuesday, March  6, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

The ladies<span class='line-break'> </span> had a meeting at Mr.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jessie Hutcherson's.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs. Booker called me<span class='line-break'> </span> and said that she had <span class='line-break'> </span> a quilt in the frames<span class='line-break'> </span> and I could help quilt<span class='line-break'> </span> if I would. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben got a package<span class='line-break'> </span> throu the mail today <span class='line-break'> </span> and a part of it is<span class='line-break'> </span> lost. He is very sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> about it.</p>

</div>

<div id="page-2333">
<h3><a name="page-2333">Wednesday, March  7, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear windy day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men did not do much<span class='line-break'> </span> work of any kind. He went with <span class='line-break'> </span> Jack Hubband to Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie got dinner and<span class='line-break'> </span> churned. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Mr. Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> and helped Mrs. Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> quilt. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard today that Mildred<span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson has pneumonia.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope that she may<span class='line-break'> </span> get well again.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had a letter from <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie. They are well<span class='line-break'> </span> now. Bend and Jim are <span class='line-break'> </span> invited to a barn<span class='line-break'> </span> raising tomorrow. <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope the wind won't <span class='line-break'> </span> blow like it has <span class='line-break'> </span> today.<span class='line-break'> </span>  </p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2335">
<h3><a name="page-2335">Thursday, March  8, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben sent<span class='line-break'> </span> John Ward to Renan this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning for a matress<span class='line-break'> </span> and shavings. Jim cleaned<span class='line-break'> </span> up a brier patch and<span class='line-break'> </span> then went to John<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutchersons to a barn<span class='line-break'> </span> raising. This morning <span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie got dinner. She<span class='line-break'> </span> made the children some <span class='line-break'> </span> pies. I went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> [Mildred Ferguson?].<span class='line-break'> </span> She is sick. Julia <span class='line-break'> </span> is worried a most to death<span class='line-break'> </span> about her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I come by Mr. Bookers <span class='line-break'> </span> and bought a few<span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes for the<span class='line-break'> </span> children.<span class='line-break'> </span> Well Ben has come <span class='line-break'> </span> to go to bed.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2334">
<h3><a name="page-2334">Friday, March  9, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the pasture<span class='line-break'> </span> fence. Ben went to Lee's<span class='line-break'> </span> to a [cutting mach?].<span class='line-break'> </span> We had [creasy salit] <span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner. The land <span class='line-break'> </span> was frozen this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went <span class='line-break'> </span> to school. I churned<span class='line-break'> </span> and baked some sweet<span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes. Afther the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come home, we shucked <span class='line-break'> </span> two shocks of corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry brought it to <span class='line-break'> </span> the corn house.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Mayhew and Eula<span class='line-break'> </span> and Harold come and <span class='line-break'> </span> they played games. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2336">
<h3><a name="page-2336">Saturday, March 10, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy windy day. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben worked on his car most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day and Jim helped<span class='line-break'> </span> him some. <span class='line-break'> </span> The children<span class='line-break'> </span> has had a good time<span class='line-break'> </span> looking on. Nellie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I put a quilt together <span class='line-break'> </span> and mended some things <span class='line-break'> </span> for the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard from Mildred.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is very sick.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs. [Kellie?] is very sick.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oh I hope they may <span class='line-break'> </span> get well. <span class='line-break'> </span> Irvin Harvey was <span class='line-break'> </span> here today for butter.<span class='line-break'> </span> He said hat he was<span class='line-break'> </span> at Ben Worsham's <span class='line-break'> </span> last night at a <span class='line-break'> </span> sosial. Frank Blair<span class='line-break'> </span> says that he is going <span class='line-break'> </span> to start west one <span class='line-break'> </span> day next week. I know<span class='line-break'> </span> they will miss him <span class='line-break'> </span> at home.</p>

<div id="page-2337">
<h3><a name="page-2337">Sunday, March 11, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Henry went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Johnson Reynolds.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mildred Ferguson is<span class='line-break'> </span> seriously sick. Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner. She baked<span class='line-break'> </span> potato pies that pleased<span class='line-break'> </span> the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben helped Edna fix <span class='line-break'> </span> her beads. Painted them<span class='line-break'> </span> for her.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna fed the calf <span class='line-break'> </span> for me. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mable is sitting up in<span class='line-break'> </span> the bed talking. She has<span class='line-break'> </span> a bunch of violets.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have stayed with the<span class='line-break'> </span> children in the dining<span class='line-break'> </span> room. Ben put papers<span class='line-break'> </span> under his mattress<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. </p>

<h3><a name="page-2338">Monday, March 12, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> helped Norman Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> make a [harrow].<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie got most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. She sewed<span class='line-break'> </span> some. <br />
<div id="page-2355">
<h3><a name="page-2355">Wednesday, March 28, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very windy day. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried Lizzie to Dr. Owen<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Mrs Owen carried<span class='line-break'> </span> her to Gretna. Jim plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> while Ben was gone. Then Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed the ballance of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Working three horses<span class='line-break'> </span> to the plow and it pulls them<span class='line-break'> </span> hard. Jim worked some<span class='line-break'> </span> on the garden. Cleaned <span class='line-break'> </span> out the spring. Raked <span class='line-break'> </span> around the spring<span class='line-break'> </span> yard and burned the <span class='line-break'> </span> trash. Henry and Edna has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin sick all day. They<span class='line-break'> </span> are broke out now and <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope they will soon<span class='line-break'> </span> be well again.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nell has waited on <span class='line-break'> </span> the children with<span class='line-break'> </span> some thing to try to eat<span class='line-break'> </span> and water to drink. She<span class='line-break'> </span> has cut out sewing<span class='line-break'> </span> but did not do much<span class='line-break'> </span> sewing today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2354">
<h3><a name="page-2354">Thursday, March 29, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear colde day. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben plowed half the<span class='line-break'> </span> day. John Ward plowed some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Renan and Cedar <span class='line-break'> </span> Forest this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> He got a plow from<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Dews. Jim plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> up the garden and planted<span class='line-break'> </span> some things. Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield is here<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. Henry and Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> are both sick. They<span class='line-break'> </span> are broke out with<span class='line-break'> </span> measles. I do hope they<span class='line-break'> </span> will be better soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> They both got a lettr<span class='line-break'> </span> from their school mates<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Nellie cut and<span class='line-break'> </span> made Mabel two<span class='line-break'> </span> dresses and bloomers<span class='line-break'> </span> today. I doged a<span class='line-break'> </span> bout as usual.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2356">
<h3><a name="page-2356">Friday, March 30, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben and Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed some. They finished<span class='line-break'> </span> hauling up the corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> John Ward planted<span class='line-break'> </span> his garden. Nellie finished<span class='line-break'> </span> making the bayby two<span class='line-break'> </span> dresses and bloomers. I worked<span class='line-break'> </span> the button holes. Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> washed all the evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> the post office in [Gretna?]<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Henry and Edna <span class='line-break'> </span> has bin sick all day. <span class='line-break'> </span> Edna is some better<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. Franklin <span class='line-break'> </span> has followed the men<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day. <span class='line-break'> </span> Our phone has gone dead.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today we cant her <span class='line-break'> </span> over it so as to under<span class='line-break'> </span> stand any thing that is <span class='line-break'> </span> said. Ben went to Norman<span class='line-break'> </span> Bookers tonight to get them<span class='line-break'> </span> to phone Johnson Reynolds<span class='line-break'> </span> to come and fix it.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2357">
<h3><a name="page-2357">Saturday, March 31, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A windy day. The ground<span class='line-break'> </span> was frozen this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> They plowed some here<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Johnson come and<span class='line-break'> </span> fixed the phone. Edna is<span class='line-break'> </span> feeling fine a gain. Henry <span class='line-break'> </span> is not so well. Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> finished Ednas dress today.<span class='line-break'> </span> She has made the <span class='line-break'> </span> baby two dresses and <span class='line-break'> </span> Edna one this week. <span class='line-break'> </span> I dont do any thing that<span class='line-break'> </span> counts but keep busy<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the time. <span class='line-break'> </span> John Ward and family <span class='line-break'> </span> went visiting this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I guess they got very<span class='line-break'> </span> colde. Mabel seemed to<span class='line-break'> </span> have a colde. I am so<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry for her to be sick.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben worked in his<span class='line-break'> </span> garden some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope it may get<span class='line-break'> </span> warmer tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> Guess the fruit is killed. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2358">
<h3><a name="page-2358">Sunday, April  1, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear colde day. Ice plenty.<span class='line-break'> </span> This morning guess the most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the fruit is killed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried Jim and Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> to the train and back by<span class='line-break'> </span> about ten oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have staid here all<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Henry come down <span class='line-break'> </span> stairs today. I hope that<span class='line-break'> </span> they may soon get well.<span class='line-break'> </span> John Hutcherson was<span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Said Mrs Jesse<span class='line-break'> </span> has measles.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry for them<span class='line-break'> </span> with that baby and <span class='line-break'> </span> no one to wait on them. <span class='line-break'> </span> I get to want to see some<span class='line-break'> </span> of the children so bad. <span class='line-break'> </span> I feel like starting <span class='line-break'> </span> but I cant go and <span class='line-break'> </span> some of them cant and <span class='line-break'> </span> wont come to see me.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2359">
<h3><a name="page-2359">Monday, April  2, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear colde day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Jim worked all <span class='line-break'> </span> day. John Ward worked<span class='line-break'> </span> half the day. Then took <span class='line-break'> </span> holiday. Kate Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see us today. I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see her. So glad<span class='line-break'> </span> she is able to walk that far.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim got home last night <span class='line-break'> </span> and we did not hear<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim. Marvin brought <span class='line-break'> </span> him. I know he had a<span class='line-break'> </span> colde trip. I would<span class='line-break'> </span> of bin glad to see him<span class='line-break'> </span> and all the rest of<span class='line-break'> </span> them. I miss Nettie.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hendricks Baley has<span class='line-break'> </span> measles. Hope it wont hurt<span class='line-break'> </span> her much.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin is sick to<span class='line-break'> </span> night. We think he is <span class='line-break'> </span> taking measles.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and Franklin and Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> did not eat supper.</p>

<div class="page-content">

Jim planted potatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie Reynolds come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see us this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad that she <span class='line-break'> </span> come. Johnson come<span class='line-break'> </span> for her. I was glad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben would of carried <span class='line-break'> </span> her but his car has<span class='line-break'> </span> no top.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franlkin is sick.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and Henry are<span class='line-break'> </span> getting on very well.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had a letter from <span class='line-break'> </span> Lottie Craddock. She <span class='line-break'> </span> staid at Posey Reynolds<span class='line-break'> </span> last night. Hope<span class='line-break'> </span> it may prove to be<span class='line-break'> </span> a good one. <span class='line-break'> </span> The children cough<span class='line-break'> </span> so bad I am sorry <span class='line-break'> </span> for them.</p>

He bougt some<span class='line-break'> </span> matches. Lelia Ward<span class='line-break'> </span> washed some for <span class='line-break'> </span> me today and ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> and brought the clothes<span class='line-break'> </span> home. There is so <span class='line-break'> </span> much that should be<span class='line-break'> </span> done that I cant do.</p>

Franklin is sick<span class='line-break'> </span> and Mabel dont feel <span class='line-break'> </span> good a bit and is so<span class='line-break'> </span> cross. She<span class='line-break'> </span> said that the most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the sick was<span class='line-break'> </span> feeling a better.<span class='line-break'> </span> I will be so glad<span class='line-break'> </span> when the measles<span class='line-break'> </span> is over. <div id="page-2371">
<h3><a name="page-2371">Friday, April 13, 1923</a></h3>

He<span class='line-break'> </span> is seven years olde today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I mended a quilt that<span class='line-break'> </span> the dogs tore. <div id="page-2370">
<h3><a name="page-2370">Saturday, April 14, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Nellie got a <span class='line-break'> </span> telagram to come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin at once as she<span class='line-break'> </span> needed her. She fixed <span class='line-break'> </span> and went this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna with her. They <span class='line-break'> </span> got home be for night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got supper and we <span class='line-break'> </span> eat by day light.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry for Nellie.<span class='line-break'> </span> I will miss her so<span class='line-break'> </span> much. She has bin <span class='line-break'> </span> so good to the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel will miss her<span class='line-break'> </span> so much. The boys saw<span class='line-break'> </span> Paul Smith. He said <span class='line-break'> </span> that Reese and Roy was<span class='line-break'> </span> sick with measles.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so sorry for<span class='line-break'> </span> them all but hope<span class='line-break'> </span> that they may get on<span class='line-break'> </span> ok. They children here<span class='line-break'> </span> seem well a gain.</p>

<br />
<div id="page-2373">
<h3><a name="page-2373">Sunday, April 15, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. We all <span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home until<span class='line-break'> </span> noon. Then Henry went<span class='line-break'> </span> to May Brumfields. He come<span class='line-break'> </span> home about sundown. <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben hunted crows<span class='line-break'> </span> nest. Foud three. Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> and Franklin and Mabel and I<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at the house. I wanted<span class='line-break'> </span> to get out but the <span class='line-break'> </span> weather is rough and colde.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lilia Ward come this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and helped to clean<span class='line-break'> </span> up some. I got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> by twelve oclock. Have<span class='line-break'> </span> some little chickens that<span class='line-break'> </span> need putting out but the <span class='line-break'> </span> weather is two bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bathed Franklin and Mabel. <span class='line-break'> </span> I told them that was<span class='line-break'> </span> the last of the measles<span class='line-break'> </span> if they dont take colde. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2372">
<h3><a name="page-2372">Monday, April 16, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear cool day. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Jim cemented a<span class='line-break'> </span> round a spring up in<span class='line-break'> </span> the field. John Ward<span class='line-break'> </span> shelled some corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> Fate[?] and Mollie and<span class='line-break'> </span> Denia come a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while Cordie come with<span class='line-break'> </span> her mother. I was so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they come. <span class='line-break'> </span> I get to want to<span class='line-break'> </span> see them all but<span class='line-break'> </span> cant. Hattie washed<span class='line-break'> </span> for me today. Lelia<span class='line-break'> </span> washed five bed quilts<span class='line-break'> </span> for me today. I am <span class='line-break'> </span> glad that washing is done.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a small check <span class='line-break'> </span> today. I am glad of <span class='line-break'> </span> that interest on <span class='line-break'> </span> my bonds. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2375">
<h3><a name="page-2375">Tuesday, April 17, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. Ben and<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim put up wire all <span class='line-break'> </span> day fencing in a pasture.<span class='line-break'> </span> John Ward went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> mill with corn. He got<span class='line-break'> </span> his grinding done. I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to get some meal.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin lone some<span class='line-break'> </span> today for some one to talk<span class='line-break'> </span> to. The baby has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> good today. She slept<span class='line-break'> </span> some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The other children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got in wood<span class='line-break'> </span> and got water <span class='line-break'> </span> and milked the cows<span class='line-break'> </span> and got supper.</p>

<div id="page-2374">
<h3><a name="page-2374">Wednesday, April 18, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear colde windy<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Ben and Jim worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on the fence some. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> made a hotbed and<span class='line-break'> </span> worked in the garden <span class='line-break'> </span> some. John Ward<span class='line-break'> </span> draged the corn land.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben got his gladolis<span class='line-break'> </span> bulbs. Jim got a letter<span class='line-break'> </span> from his son inlaw<span class='line-break'> </span> telling that Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> was feeling better<span class='line-break'> </span> and that Nellie got<span class='line-break'> </span> to Silver Grove Sunday.<span class='line-break'> </span> The three children <span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel and I have a bad<span class='line-break'> </span> day. It was so colde<span class='line-break'> </span> that she could not<span class='line-break'> </span> stay out of doors and<span class='line-break'> </span> that was what whe<span class='line-break'> </span> wanted to do. I think<span class='line-break'> </span> now that I will enjoy<span class='line-break'> </span> warm weather. Edna <span class='line-break'> </span> has come to go to bed.</p>

<div id="page-2377">
<h3><a name="page-2377">Thursday, April 19, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Jim planted<span class='line-break'> </span> some in the garden.<span class='line-break'> </span> I planted some <span class='line-break'> </span> dahlias. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel staid out<span class='line-break'> </span> doors most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day. I got breakfast<span class='line-break'> </span> and milked the cows.<span class='line-break'> </span> Emthied[?] the milk<span class='line-break'> </span> and churned. Fed the <span class='line-break'> </span> chickens and got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and washed <span class='line-break'> </span> the dishes and rocked<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel to sleep and <span class='line-break'> </span> read the paper some<span class='line-break'> </span> and fed the chickens<span class='line-break'> </span> and milked the cows<span class='line-break'> </span> and got supper and<span class='line-break'> </span> washed dishes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Now we are ready<span class='line-break'> </span> to go to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have to stay here so close<span class='line-break'> </span> that I dont know anything<span class='line-break'> </span> to write. </p>

They<span class='line-break'> </span> had a fish fry. There <span class='line-break'> </span> was some fifty or more<span class='line-break'> </span> people there. The me<span class='line-break'> </span> done the cooking. The <span class='line-break'> </span> fish was fried as nice<span class='line-break'> </span> as could be. We had<span class='line-break'> </span> a good time. <div id="page-2390">
<h3><a name="page-2390">Friday, May  4, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.<span class='line-break'> </span> They finished planting<span class='line-break'> </span> corn here today and<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed some for tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> school house to practice<span class='line-break'> </span> for a play to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and Edna walked <span class='line-break'> </span> over there tonight. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and Franklin went<span class='line-break'> </span> after dark on the <span class='line-break'> </span> machine. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they went. He<span class='line-break'> </span> will bring them all home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and the baby and I<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home. I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to sleep and made this<span class='line-break'> </span> mark. The children and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Norman<span class='line-break'> </span> Bookers. We had a <span class='line-break'> </span> pleasant visit.<span class='line-break'> </span> There is several places<span class='line-break'> </span> that I would like to<span class='line-break'> </span> go but can't.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2393">
<h3><a name="page-2393">Saturday, May  5, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks plowed and worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on the land until twelve<span class='line-break'> </span> oclock. Then Ben carried <span class='line-break'> </span> the children and I <span class='line-break'> </span> to White Falls fishing.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did not catch <span class='line-break'> </span> any thing any acount.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had a good trip any<span class='line-break'> </span> way. Tonight Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> the children to Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone to a show. Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> is a sleep now.<span class='line-break'> </span> While I was gone<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate and Irvin Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come. I wish I had <span class='line-break'> </span> not gone. Jim worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in the garden some.<span class='line-break'> </span> They moved the pigs<span class='line-break'> </span> to a new lot today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I did not milk the<span class='line-break'> </span> cows tonight. I had<span class='line-break'> </span> early supper.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2392">
<h3><a name="page-2392">Sunday, May  6, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Gretna this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning to take the train<span class='line-break'> </span> to go to the lodge in <span class='line-break'> </span> Tennessee. I do hope he<span class='line-break'> </span> may make the trip o.k.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> Sunday School this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> The rest of us staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home until after twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and Franklin and Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to Mr.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons. John and Sarah<span class='line-break'> </span> Emerson and three children<span class='line-break'> </span> and Mr. Trent come here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Walter Emerson come<span class='line-break'> </span> for me to come.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them. I get so lonesome<span class='line-break'> </span> I cant hardly stay<span class='line-break'> </span> at home. Henry has <span class='line-break'> </span> gone to Uncle Johnson <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols to carrie Floids<span class='line-break'> </span> [cap/car?] home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2394">
<h3><a name="page-2394">Monday, May  7, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Jim hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> olde rails to the wood<span class='line-break'> </span> pile for stove wood.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry plowed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie Gilbert washed<span class='line-break'> </span> here. Lelia Ward<span class='line-break'> </span> come here a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while. She brought<span class='line-break'> </span> all of her children<span class='line-break'> </span> with her. Good looking<span class='line-break'> </span> little darkeys.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin busy<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children and I<span class='line-break'> </span> walked over to the<span class='line-break'> </span> barns looking for<span class='line-break'> </span> wilde straw berrie<span class='line-break'> </span> blooms. Found a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> little patch.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2395">
<h3><a name="page-2395">Tuesday, May  8, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Jim and <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and John Ward put<span class='line-break'> </span> in fertilizer an fixed<span class='line-break'> </span> some land ready for planting.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Johnson <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and Mabel went <span class='line-break'> </span> to the store. Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> got some tobacco for<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and a box of paper <span class='line-break'> </span> for me. Mollie walked <span class='line-break'> </span> with us part way<span class='line-break'> </span> home. Mr. and Mrs. <span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons come on their <span class='line-break'> </span> car and taken us on. I <span class='line-break'> </span> was glad. Mrs Edmons<span class='line-break'> </span> had bin to see her<span class='line-break'> </span> great grand son. He <span class='line-break'> </span> was born last night. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Elders son.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin played all<span class='line-break'> </span> the evening with Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> Farthing.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2396">
<h3><a name="page-2396">Wednesday, May  9, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A windy day and colde.<span class='line-break'> </span> The coldest that I ever <span class='line-break'> </span> saw for the time of year.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am a fraid that all<span class='line-break'> </span> green things will be killed.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had storm last night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rain and wind. I am glad it was<span class='line-break'> </span> no worse. The men put in <span class='line-break'> </span> fertilizer this morning. <span class='line-break'> </span> It has bein so colde and<span class='line-break'> </span> windy that they have not <span class='line-break'> </span> done much of any thing <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> got a note from her <span class='line-break'> </span> daddy this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope he may get<span class='line-break'> </span> home tomorrow. I have<span class='line-break'> </span> milked, cooked, and churned,<span class='line-break'> </span> parched coffee and <span class='line-break'> </span> done nothing all day. <span class='line-break'> </span> Daysie the dog is<span class='line-break'> </span> missing tonight. I am<span class='line-break'> </span> afraid some one has<span class='line-break'> </span> killed her. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2397">
<h3><a name="page-2397">Thursday, May 10, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde day. Some <span class='line-break'> </span> frost this morning. Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> has got home. The chilen <span class='line-break'> </span> and I are as glad as <span class='line-break'> </span> can be. Jim has worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on the garden most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day. Heard today<span class='line-break'> </span> that little Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith is in the hosptille<span class='line-break'> </span> at Roanoke. The little<span class='line-break'> </span> girls is at Kate Harveys.<span class='line-break'> </span> Arch Moons son <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim killed him self<span class='line-break'> </span> last night at Cedar<span class='line-break'> </span> Forest Bridge. Was found<span class='line-break'> </span> in the creek this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> He ran his car on<span class='line-break'> </span> the bank of the creek <span class='line-break'> </span> and he fell in the creek.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben brought all of <span class='line-break'> </span> the children a<span class='line-break'> </span> little present. They<span class='line-break'> </span> are glad and I am<span class='line-break'> </span> two. They found Daisy<span class='line-break'> </span> dead this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2399">
<h3><a name="page-2399">Friday, May 11, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cool windy day. Frost <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning , enough to kill<span class='line-break'> </span> some things. The men sawed<span class='line-break'> </span> wood here today. Good stove <span class='line-break'> </span> wood. Heard today that <span class='line-break'> </span> Claud Edmons killed the dog.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard from Marvins Carrie[?] <span class='line-break'> </span> come home yesterday. The <span class='line-break'> </span> baby is no better.<span class='line-break'> </span> Solde my cow that I<span class='line-break'> </span> called Spot for $35[?].<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Henry went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna today. Ben bought<span class='line-break'> </span> meal and brand and sugar. <span class='line-break'> </span> I coud of went but<span class='line-break'> </span> the wind blowed so <span class='line-break'> </span> hard that I did not<span class='line-break'> </span> want to go.<span class='line-break'> </span> I want to see all of<span class='line-break'> </span> the children but can't.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2398">
<h3><a name="page-2398">Saturday, May 12, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A windy day. We need<span class='line-break'> </span> rain bad. The men have<span class='line-break'> </span> not done much today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not done <span class='line-break'> </span> any thing to count<span class='line-break'> </span> any thing. Lelia<span class='line-break'> </span> Ward come this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and washed up the<span class='line-break'> </span> dishes for me.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs. Booker come <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening to get<span class='line-break'> </span> a setting of eggs<span class='line-break'> </span> for Mrs. Dave Booker[?].<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Henry <span class='line-break'> </span> are fixing to go<span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone<span class='line-break'> </span> to the Lodge.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim planted some <span class='line-break'> </span> tomatoe plants.<span class='line-break'> </span> The weather is so<span class='line-break'> </span> colde and the land <span class='line-break'> </span> so dry that nothing<span class='line-break'> </span> cant grow. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> is worrying me. They won't<span class='line-break'> </span> go to sleep.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2401">
<h3><a name="page-2401">Sunday, May 13, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little rain this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is badly needed.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all was at home at<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Ben carried the<span class='line-break'> </span> children to see Grandma<span class='line-break'> </span> Carr. I went to Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harveys. Charles and wife was<span class='line-break'> </span> there. Pearl and Mrs Wiggins[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> come. Reese Smith<span class='line-break'> </span> come and brought the<span class='line-break'> </span> little girls. Reese and <span class='line-break'> </span> Paul and Roy come down <span class='line-break'> </span> here. I come with them. <span class='line-break'> </span> I let them have <span class='line-break'> </span> some butter. <span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson and Mollie and<span class='line-break'> </span> Christine come and<span class='line-break'> </span> staid a little while. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> got home about dark.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had supper ready.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2400">
<h3><a name="page-2400">Monday, May 14, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> land most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oh how I wist we<span class='line-break'> </span> could have rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have felt bad<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. Guess <span class='line-break'> </span> walking up to Renan<span class='line-break'> </span> had something to do<span class='line-break'> </span> with my bad feelings. <span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin busy<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. Cleaned <span class='line-break'> </span> up the chickens coop.<span class='line-break'> </span> I gathered a few<span class='line-break'> </span> strawberries today. The<span class='line-break'> </span> first that has ripened<span class='line-break'> </span> this spring. Lelia Ward<span class='line-break'> </span> sent me some salit<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner. I fried<span class='line-break'> </span> some pies this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben is very much<span class='line-break'> </span> comnplaining tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> He has a very bad colde.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim had a letter from <span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie today. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2402">
<h3><a name="page-2402">Tuesday, May 15, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. We had<span class='line-break'> </span> a shower of rain this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. They got ready <span class='line-break'> </span> to water their plant <span class='line-break'> </span> beds then did not because<span class='line-break'> </span> it rained. Some they picked <span class='line-break'> </span> weeds until night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went with Mrs booker<span class='line-break'> </span> to see Mrs Elder[?].<span class='line-break'> </span> She has a fine little <span class='line-break'> </span> boy. Henry caught<span class='line-break'> </span> a perch and an elle <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. I skined <span class='line-break'> </span> the eel with Ednas <span class='line-break'> </span> help.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wrote and sent<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie a letter this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. I hope to<span class='line-break'> </span> hear from carrie soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2403">
<h3><a name="page-2403">Wednesday, May 16, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning. We<span class='line-break'> </span> were glad. The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> planted some tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> but it is colde. I am a<span class='line-break'> </span> fraid it will die.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Booker helpe them. <span class='line-break'> </span> His plants were not ready<span class='line-break'> </span> to plant. I made a<span class='line-break'> </span> tick for a bed. Will <span class='line-break'> </span> put feathers in it<span class='line-break'> </span> soon if nothings.<span class='line-break'> </span> I dont know any thing<span class='line-break'> </span> to write. I want to see <span class='line-break'> </span> all of the <span class='line-break'> </span> children. I get lonesome<span class='line-break'> </span> and worrie a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> what is to do and how<span class='line-break'> </span> to do it.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2404">
<h3><a name="page-2404">Thursday, May 17, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cool windy day. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben worked on their<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco ground getting it<span class='line-break'> </span> ready to plant. <span class='line-break'> </span> I baked a pudding and got<span class='line-break'> </span> a few strawberries for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Have not done<span class='line-break'> </span> much of anything this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening. I have not felt<span class='line-break'> </span> well all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did not get any mail <span class='line-break'> </span> today. Thre was a wreck <span class='line-break'> </span> between Lynchburg and<span class='line-break'> </span> the island.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went to Renan this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. Heard that they <span class='line-break'> </span> had sent Mr. Tiny[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Shelton to Stanton. His<span class='line-break'> </span> mind has got bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry calls. He has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> gigging. All the rest<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to bed.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2405">
<h3><a name="page-2405">Friday, May 18, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. A little rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on tobacco land. Hattie<span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today. The clothes<span class='line-break'> </span> dried quick. I made two<span class='line-break'> </span> pillow tick and one bolster<span class='line-break'> </span> tick and filled them <span class='line-break'> </span> with feathers and a bed <span class='line-break'> </span> tick. I am so glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> is done. Irvin Harvey and<span class='line-break'> </span> Hazel and Eva Smith come<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We heard that Carries<span class='line-break'> </span> baby was opperated on. <span class='line-break'> </span> We dont know what<span class='line-break'> </span> was the matter with it.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children has<span class='line-break'> </span> played and bin good<span class='line-break'> </span> as I could ask.<span class='line-break'> </span> We picked a few<span class='line-break'> </span> straw berries this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> some dew berries.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were all eat.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2406">
<h3><a name="page-2406">Saturday, May 19, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on tobacco land. Jim planted<span class='line-break'> </span> some sweet potatoe slips.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ray Booker come for some<span class='line-break'> </span> musk mellon seed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and all of her children<span class='line-break'> </span> come and Kate Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> with them. I was so <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see them. Little<span class='line-break'> </span> Julia has fallen off but<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope she may get well. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone. There was not<span class='line-break'> </span> any preaching.<span class='line-break'> </span> The baby has a sore eye.<span class='line-break'> </span> A sty coming I think.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and Lawson Emerson<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone giggin to<span class='line-break'> </span> night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2407">
<h3><a name="page-2407">Sunday, May 20, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning. Rain this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening. We are glad of rain. <span class='line-break'> </span> Lawson Emerson staid here<span class='line-break'> </span> last night after they quit<span class='line-break'> </span> fishing. They caught three<span class='line-break'> </span> eels. Henry and Lawson skined<span class='line-break'> </span> them and had them ready to<span class='line-break'> </span> cook for breakfast. They went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Sunday school and <span class='line-break'> </span> home for dinner. Ben and <span class='line-break'> </span> Edna went to preaching <span class='line-break'> </span> at Strait Stone. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried the children<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr. Powers. Mrs Power<span class='line-break'> </span> was not at home. They<span class='line-break'> </span> come home through the rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went to John<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutchersons. While he was <span class='line-break'> </span> over there Will Thomas<span class='line-break'> </span> Davis shot at Will<span class='line-break'> </span> Dickerson. Hit Bettie Davis.<span class='line-break'> </span> A bad thing for Bob Starkey<span class='line-break'> </span> as they were his hands.<span class='line-break'> </span> To work Bettie was staying<span class='line-break'> </span> with Mrs Elder.<span class='line-break'> </span> Killed my chickens to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2408">
<h3><a name="page-2408">Monday, May 21, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben and Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> and all that could drop or <span class='line-break'> </span> plant tobacco went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> field. Mabel staid out all <span class='line-break'> </span> day for her first time. She<span class='line-break'> </span> had a good time playing. Lelia<span class='line-break'> </span> Ward and her children was at the<span class='line-break'> </span> field this evening. I churned<span class='line-break'> </span> and got dinner. Fried some <span class='line-break'> </span> nice meat and had Irish potatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Stewed some apples and<span class='line-break'> </span> picked some strawberries.<span class='line-break'> </span> Baked corn and wheat <span class='line-break'> </span> bread. Have not seen any<span class='line-break'> </span> one to day to hear any news.<span class='line-break'> </span> I planted a few beet plants<span class='line-break'> </span> in the garden.<span class='line-break'> </span> Found one of my hens<span class='line-break'> </span> dead this morning. <span class='line-break'> </span> The first poppy bloomed<span class='line-break'> </span> today. It is beautiful. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2409">
<h3><a name="page-2409">Tuesday, May 22, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. the men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the tobacco land<span class='line-break'> </span> except Ben. He went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Chatham to be on a jury.<span class='line-break'> </span> He did not want to go<span class='line-break'> </span> but could not get off. <span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie washed here<span class='line-break'> </span> today. I and three<span class='line-break'> </span> children went to George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blains. Denia was not<span class='line-break'> </span> at home. She had gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to Otho Blains to <span class='line-break'> </span> carrie Sallie some <span class='line-break'> </span> straw berries. They<span class='line-break'> </span> said that they had<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered 9 gallons at<span class='line-break'> </span> one time. Cordie had<span class='line-break'> </span> had some beautiful<span class='line-break'> </span> sweat peas. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2410">
<h3><a name="page-2410">Wednesday, May 23, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. A little rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. We need more<span class='line-break'> </span> so bad. It is very cold for<span class='line-break'> </span> May. We have had a fire all<span class='line-break'> </span> the evening. I got a letter<span class='line-break'> </span> from Nellie today telling<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout Evylins little baby. <span class='line-break'> </span> It was born the 20th of the<span class='line-break'> </span> month. It is named Elain. <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to hear from<span class='line-break'> </span> her. Hope she may do well. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has not come home<span class='line-break'> </span> yet. I know he is put<span class='line-break'> </span> out about having to stay.<span class='line-break'> </span> They have bin fixing land<span class='line-break'> </span> ready to plant all day<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Jim went to <span class='line-break'> </span> John Hutchersons plant<span class='line-break'> </span> bed and got tomatoe<span class='line-break'> </span> and pepper plants and planted<span class='line-break'> </span> them. Then he planted <span class='line-break'> </span> some water mellon <span class='line-break'> </span> seed. We had early <span class='line-break'> </span> supper tonight. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2411">
<h3><a name="page-2411">Thursday, May 24, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. No rain<span class='line-break'> </span> to do any good. The folks<span class='line-break'> </span> planted tobacco half<span class='line-break'> </span> the day. They plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> in the corn this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim planted potatoe slips.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was disapointed<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. I wanted <span class='line-break'> </span> to go to [Ehels?] but had<span class='line-break'> </span> no way to go. Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker went on the<span class='line-break'> </span> buggy. I got [Beaulas?]<span class='line-break'> </span> babyes picture. She is<span class='line-break'> </span> pretty. I was glad of<span class='line-break'> </span> the picture. Glad to be<span class='line-break'> </span> remembered.<span class='line-break'> </span> I sewed a little this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. We need a <span class='line-break'> </span> lot of sewing here<span class='line-break'> </span> but I dont know<span class='line-break'> </span> how it is to get<span class='line-break'> </span> done. Jim got a letter<span class='line-break'> </span> from Nel to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children brought a <span class='line-break'> </span> little chicken home today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2412">
<h3><a name="page-2412">Saturday, May 26, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men has<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed a little. Worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> the car some. Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone for some<span class='line-break'> </span> thing for the car. Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben and Lawson Emerson <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone gigging to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim is at the dining <span class='line-break'> </span> room reading. Three of<span class='line-break'> </span> the children has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to bed. I have wanted <span class='line-break'> </span> to go some where to <span class='line-break'> </span> fish but cant go. No <span class='line-break'> </span> one will take me. I <span class='line-break'> </span> could go most any <span class='line-break'> </span> evening if I had away.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think it is right to <span class='line-break'> </span> work but I think it<span class='line-break'> </span> is hard for me to stay<span class='line-break'> </span> right here all the time. <span class='line-break'> </span> Thas it what suits <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben. I dont know <span class='line-break'> </span> anything to write so I will <span class='line-break'> </span> [g?] some. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ednas cat is sick. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2413">
<h3><a name="page-2413">Friday, May 25, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. No rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> We need rain so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben plowed in the corn<span class='line-break'> </span> and Henry replanted<span class='line-break'> </span> and they both quareled <span class='line-break'> </span> because it is so sorry. <span class='line-break'> </span> The three children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson Reynolds.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie was makeing<span class='line-break'> </span> [Christine?] a dress.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had Alcie Callans<span class='line-break'> </span> there. She was ironing.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey and Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith and children come. <span class='line-break'> </span> I was so glad that <span class='line-break'> </span> they come. Julia can <span class='line-break'> </span> walk a gain. I am <span class='line-break'> </span> very glad. [Reise?] <span class='line-break'> </span> brought us home. That<span class='line-break'> </span> helped so much. <span class='line-break'> </span> I had a hen for dinner. <span class='line-break'> </span> I will quit. I am a sleep<span class='line-break'> </span> or about that.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ednas cat is sick tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2414">
<h3><a name="page-2414">Monday, May 28, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Chatham. Thomson<span class='line-break'> </span> carried him. Jim and Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> and John watered the<span class='line-break'> </span> plant bed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate and Irvin come a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening. The girls has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin dressed like boys<span class='line-break'> </span> and played all the<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. I filled <span class='line-break'> </span> some pillow ticks<span class='line-break'> </span> with feathers this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. Did not get<span class='line-break'> </span> the washing done<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Hatties folks<span class='line-break'> </span> has the measles. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to Renan<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning fo sugar.<span class='line-break'> </span> I made three quarts<span class='line-break'> </span> of straw berry preserves<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. <span class='line-break'> </span> We need rain very bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did hope we would have some <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2415">
<h3><a name="page-2415">Sunday, May 27, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. We need rain<span class='line-break'> </span> very bad. We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until after dinner. <span class='line-break'> </span> Then Ben and Henry and Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Strait Stone.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had a Sunday school <span class='line-break'> </span> convention there this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went to look for <span class='line-break'> </span> straw berries. He foun a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> lot. Franklin and Mabel and<span class='line-break'> </span> I staid at home. No one<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim was carrieing water<span class='line-break'> </span> to the garden. Mabel was <span class='line-break'> </span> with him. He helped her<span class='line-break'> </span> across the branch and <span class='line-break'> </span> sliped and fell in the<span class='line-break'> </span> branch. Got almost <span class='line-break'> </span> wet all over.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went with Floid Renyolds home<span class='line-break'> </span> and have not come<span class='line-break'> </span> home yet.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2416">
<h3><a name="page-2416">Tuesday, May 29, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben and Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> and Jim helped Mr. <span class='line-break'> </span> Booker plant tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Watered and planted.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin very<span class='line-break'> </span> busy to day. I killed<span class='line-break'> </span> and fried two chickens<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner. It is a hard <span class='line-break'> </span> time to get any thing but<span class='line-break'> </span> meat and bread.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie and Alma Bennett<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I certainly was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> thay they come. Lizzie <span class='line-break'> </span> has the tooth ache.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie brought Denia<span class='line-break'> </span> some flower [slips?].<span class='line-break'> </span> I let Edna and Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> go and carrie them <span class='line-break'> </span> home.</p>

<div id="page-2417">
<h3><a name="page-2417">Wednesday, May 30, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Some clouds<span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain. We need <span class='line-break'> </span> rain so bad. I hope it may<span class='line-break'> </span> rain very soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men spent the day<span class='line-break'> </span> hauling water and put <span class='line-break'> </span> it on their plant beds.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children has bin <span class='line-break'> </span> good today. They are all<span class='line-break'> </span> a sleep in the same<span class='line-break'> </span> bed. That is the three <span class='line-break'> </span> that stays at the<span class='line-break'> </span> house. I finished fixing <span class='line-break'> </span> the pillows that I have<span class='line-break'> </span> made ticks for. I made<span class='line-break'> </span> six. Put feathers that<span class='line-break'> </span> was in Josies bed in<span class='line-break'> </span> some of them. I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that is done. Ben worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on his car some today. <span class='line-break'> </span> I think it will run now.<span class='line-break'> </span> I can't get to go any<span class='line-break'> </span> where. That is the way<span class='line-break'> </span> that the boys want me<span class='line-break'> </span> to be.</p>

<div id="page-2418">

Peggie<span class='line-break'> </span> was in <a href='../subjects/8608' title='Mr Bookers'>Mr Bookers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> pasture. <div id="page-2425">
<h3><a name="page-2425">Thursday, June  7, 1923</a></h3>

<div id="page-2427">
<h3><a name="page-2427">Friday, June  8, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A windy day. Very hard<span class='line-break'> </span> on the crop. Mr. Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> planted tobacco but it can't <span class='line-break'> </span> live long unless it rains.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got peas to day and cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> beans. It is a hard time<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout something good<span class='line-break'> </span> to cook. I want to be<span class='line-break'> </span> thankful that we are doing<span class='line-break'> </span> as well as we are.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey and Pearl<span class='line-break'> </span> Wiggenton come a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while. Pearl brought<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel a nice dress. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs. Car sent Edna <span class='line-break'> </span> a nice dress. I am <span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they have got<span class='line-break'> </span> them. John Ward<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Level Run<span class='line-break'> </span> to a burial.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel slept a good nap<span class='line-break'> </span> in the [s?ing] and have bein<span class='line-break'> </span> good ever since.<span class='line-break'> </span> Went to sleep.</p>
