<br />
<div id="page-2501">
<h3><a name="page-2501">Friday, August 17, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and some<span class='line-break'> </span> rain. Not enough to stop<span class='line-break'> </span> work. The men suckered<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco. Jimm went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone to get the<span class='line-break'> </span> horses shod and flue<span class='line-break'> </span> joints. Got dinner. Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> caned some tomatoes <span class='line-break'> </span> and gathered some grapes.<span class='line-break'> </span> We staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> and I have no news.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lelia Ward went to a <span class='line-break'> </span> lodge meeting. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel got a letter<span class='line-break'> </span> from Edna to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got one from Kitty <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols. I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to hear from any<span class='line-break'> </span> of them. I want to <span class='line-break'> </span> go for Edna tomorrow<span class='line-break'> </span> but the men is so <span class='line-break'> </span> busy I am afraid they wont<span class='line-break'> </span> go. Fraklin and Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> has bad colds.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2500">
<h3><a name="page-2500">Saturday, August 18, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. No rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men suckered<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day. Norman<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker helped them a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Nellie and I <span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner. Nellie bathed<span class='line-break'> </span> the children. I killed two<span class='line-break'> </span> chickens and dressed them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wanted to go to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> but could not get off. <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope it may be good<span class='line-break'> </span> enough that we can<span class='line-break'> </span> go in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Floid Reynols and<span class='line-break'> </span> Stuart Owen come here<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight to see Henry.<span class='line-break'> </span> I reckon<span class='line-break'> </span> we have lots of water <span class='line-break'> </span> mellons now. <span class='line-break'> </span> I gathered a basket of<span class='line-break'> </span> tomatoes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think that the children <span class='line-break'> </span> are feeling better today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2503">
<h3><a name="page-2503">Sunday, August 19, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben and [sic] staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day. Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner. Jim went <span class='line-break'> </span> to John Hutchersons a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went bathing.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oscar Brumfield <span class='line-break'> </span> come after me and <span class='line-break'> </span> spent the day at Lees.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had a pleasant day.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had company<span class='line-break'> </span> at Lees. Lawson and <span class='line-break'> </span> Fanny Power and several <span class='line-break'> </span> others young folks and<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. and Mrs. John Will<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey.<span class='line-break'> </span> Floid Reynols brought <span class='line-break'> </span> me home. Oscar<span class='line-break'> </span> Lawson Power went<span class='line-break'> </span> off some where<span class='line-break'> </span> and had not got<span class='line-break'> </span> back when I<span class='line-break'> </span> come a way.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2502">
<h3><a name="page-2502">Monday, August 20, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Henry and John<span class='line-break'> </span> Ward suckered tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has bin sick all<span class='line-break'> </span> day. He was taken sick<span class='line-break'> </span> in the night last night<span class='line-break'> </span> and has bin sick all<span class='line-break'> </span> day. He is some better <span class='line-break'> </span> now. Claud Fitz and<span class='line-break'> </span> family come here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Norman Booker went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Gretna for the them. He<span class='line-break'> </span> brought Edna home<span class='line-break'> </span> from Marvin Smiths.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie went with <span class='line-break'> </span> him for them. They have <span class='line-break'> </span> a nice baby.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have a lot of <span class='line-break'> </span> water mellons now<span class='line-break'> </span> and see that<span class='line-break'> </span> every one enjoys<span class='line-break'> </span> then.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2505">
<h3><a name="page-2505">Tuesday, August 21, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very <span class='line-break'> </span> hot. Ben is not able to<span class='line-break'> </span> work today. He brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me to Gretna and to <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel come with us. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried Nellies trunk<span class='line-break'> </span> home. Jim and Claud <span class='line-break'> </span> Fitz was comeing from<span class='line-break'> </span> the store. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin went to Mr.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bookers. Booker commenced <span class='line-break'> </span> to cut tobacco today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry B. and John Ward<span class='line-break'> </span> helped him. Lee Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> is at Marvins. Tonight <span class='line-break'> </span> he is trying to find<span class='line-break'> </span> out a bout the <span class='line-break'> </span> election. Carrie was<span class='line-break'> </span> makeing some <span class='line-break'> </span> jellie this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She has peaches<span class='line-break'> </span> to can. She has nice snaps.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2504">
<h3><a name="page-2504">Wednesday, August 22, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning. Rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and so colde<span class='line-break'> </span> that we need fire. Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> went from here this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and Marvin went with<span class='line-break'> </span> him. I peeled peaches<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day. Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> made four gallons of<span class='line-break'> </span> preserves today. Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered the peaches.<span class='line-break'> </span> The first or nearly the <span class='line-break'> </span> first things that I done<span class='line-break'> </span> today was to spill the<span class='line-break'> </span> ink and got some<span class='line-break'> </span> on my book.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin got home a <span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes a go. He<span class='line-break'> </span> had not had his dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I certainly wish that <span class='line-break'> </span> I could know how <span class='line-break'> </span> the rain was at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am a fraid there was<span class='line-break'> </span> hail in the cloud.<span class='line-break'> </span> It has got [se?] cool.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2507">
<h3><a name="page-2507">Thursday, August 23, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day until late.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening it <a href='../subjects/7644' title='clearing land'>cleared</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> way. It has bin <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day. We have had a <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day. I peeled a lot<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> preserved them. She <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a> staid here<span class='line-break'> </span> a gain last night. I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad for him to be<span class='line-break'> </span> here. The <a href='../subjects/233' title='roads'>roads</a> was so<span class='line-break'> </span> mudy I was a fraid<span class='line-break'> </span> some thing would happen<span class='line-break'> </span> to him. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> this morning. She <span class='line-break'> </span> said that they were<span class='line-break'> </span> all <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a> at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am anxious a bout <span class='line-break'> </span> them at home. <span class='line-break'> </span> I want to know how <span class='line-break'> </span> they are getting on.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2506">
<h3><a name="page-2506">Friday, August 24, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Very cool<span class='line-break'> </span> for August. Marvin and Carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> washed this morning. I <span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner. Cooked snaps<span class='line-break'> </span> and potatoes and fried<span class='line-break'> </span> chicken. Carrie churned<span class='line-break'> </span> when she got thru washing.<span class='line-break'> </span> We went to Tim <span class='line-break'> </span> Bennetts this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and all the<span class='line-break'> </span> children and I found <span class='line-break'> </span> them all well.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lonnie Bennett was<span class='line-break'> </span> at home. <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see <span class='line-break'> </span> them all. <span class='line-break'> </span> [C?arley] Harvey and Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> was here this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while. Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> had some nice mellons<span class='line-break'> </span> and peaches. They enjoyed<span class='line-break'> </span> them. They got a <span class='line-break'> </span> bucket of snaps.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad that they come.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2508">
<h3><a name="page-2508">Saturday, August 25, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day. I am<span class='line-break'> </span> at home tonight. Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> brought me home this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning. Found them <span class='line-break'> </span> all getting on well. <span class='line-break'> </span> Some of them said<span class='line-break'> </span> that they did not<span class='line-break'> </span> miss me. I milked<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. Franklin helped<span class='line-break'> </span> me what he could. <span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks are fixing<span class='line-break'> </span> to opossome hunting.<span class='line-break'> </span> Evelyn is going two for<span class='line-break'> </span> the lack of sence.<span class='line-break'> </span> She claims to be not<span class='line-break'> </span> able to work. After <span class='line-break'> </span> this she needs no pitty<span class='line-break'> </span> only because she has<span class='line-break'> </span> no more sence.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Mayhew come<span class='line-break'> </span> up here today and <span class='line-break'> </span> got some mellons. <span class='line-break'> </span> They have a lot of them<span class='line-break'> </span> here now.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2509">
<h3><a name="page-2509">Sunday, August 26, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. We were<span class='line-break'> </span> all at home at dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> After dinner Ben and the<span class='line-break'> </span> children and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Jim Powers. Found<span class='line-break'> </span> all well except Mrs. Power.<span class='line-break'> </span> She was in bed. I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> she may get well soon. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ms Car was there. I <span class='line-break'> </span> was glad to see them<span class='line-break'> </span> all. We heard that<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs. Cotham has a son.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried a few<span class='line-break'> </span> mellons. They seemed <span class='line-break'> </span> to enjoy them. <span class='line-break'> </span> The possome hunters<span class='line-break'> </span> got in this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> about three oclock. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry is a most<span class='line-break'> </span> part going. He has <span class='line-break'> </span> a very bad colde.<span class='line-break'> </span> We stopped at Vaugn's<span class='line-break'> </span> store a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.Bought soap.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2510">
<h3><a name="page-2510">Monday, August 27, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. I am at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a gain. Lee brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me this morning. Claud<span class='line-break'> </span> Fitz started from our house<span class='line-break'> </span> to Clifton Forge today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lee brought him to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> The boys at home commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> cutting tobacco today. Norman<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker helped them. I <span class='line-break'> </span> wish I knowed how they<span class='line-break'> </span> got a long. Nellie and Evelyn<span class='line-break'> </span> will do the work if the[sic]<span class='line-break'> </span> can. Nellie has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> good to the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are pleased to stay<span class='line-break'> </span> with them when I am<span class='line-break'> </span> gone. Heard this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> that Oscar Eades and Lester<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey got hurt with<span class='line-break'> </span> a motercicle some<span class='line-break'> </span> where near Strait Stone.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope they may get<span class='line-break'> </span> well soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie has bin sewing today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2511">
<h3><a name="page-2511">Tuesday, August 28, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some<span class='line-break'> </span> rain. <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and Hollie <span class='line-break'> </span> and Richards <a href='../subjects/8856' title='cutting tobacco'>cut a <span class='line-break'> </span> cureing of tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wish I knowed<span class='line-break'> </span> what they done at<span class='line-break'> </span> home. <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> made<span class='line-break'> </span> four <a href='../subjects/9095' title='waist'>waists</a> today. I <span class='line-break'> </span> worked <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> three. I got most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> cooked.<span class='line-break'> </span> Snaps and <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> stewed <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>. We <span class='line-break'> </span> had <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> and <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>cream</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The first I had seen <span class='line-break'> </span> in a long time.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8857' title='Mrs Hollie'>Mrs Hollie</a> come this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening with her <span class='line-break'> </span> three children.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy Smith</a> gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> for tomorrow<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. I gathered <span class='line-break'> </span> butter beans.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2512">
<h3><a name="page-2512">Wednesday, August 29, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/9394' title='good'>good</a> day. A little <span class='line-break'> </span> rain. Could work most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the time. <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> made<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a> and <a href='../subjects/7635' title='pickles'>pickles</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I peeled the <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> got most of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some. <span class='line-break'> </span> I worked the button <span class='line-break'> </span> holes in two <a href='../subjects/7892' title='blouses'>blouses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> home this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were all <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> fireing on some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr McLau[gh]lins</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> She though[t] that<span class='line-break'> </span> she would invite<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8732' title='Mrs. McLau[gh]lin'>Mrs. McLau[gh]lin</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> come and spend<span class='line-break'> </span> the day but there <span class='line-break'> </span> was no one at home. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2513">
<h3><a name="page-2513">Thursday, August 30, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> washed this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. Snaps<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe</a> <a href='../subjects/46' title='pudding'>pudding</a>. I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> A colored woman came<span class='line-break'> </span> and gathered the <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Some three or 4 bushels.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried me to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> and to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Jenia Brumfield. She<span class='line-break'> </span> had come to see me.<span class='line-break'> </span> I come back with <span class='line-break'> </span> Reese. Little <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and a <a href='../subjects/7590' title='Miss Angle'>Miss Angle</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come with us home. <span class='line-break'> </span> They had <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellon</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7247' title='muskmelon'>musk mellon</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a>. All they would<span class='line-break'> </span> eat. Reese carried <span class='line-break'> </span> them home. Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Finished one of Rays<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7892' title='blouses'>blouses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2515">
<h3><a name="page-2515">Friday, August 31, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> has worked on tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. Carrie sewed<span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning. I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. This evening I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Gretna with <span class='line-break'> </span> Reese. I bought 4 dolls.<span class='line-break'> </span> Two for Carries girls.<span class='line-break'> </span> Two for Bens girls.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had a scare this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. Eva fell off<span class='line-break'> </span> the runing board of <span class='line-break'> </span> the car and Reese ran <span class='line-break'> </span> partly over her. She<span class='line-break'> </span> was hurt but not<span class='line-break'> </span> very bad. Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Lonny and [Alma?]<span class='line-break'> </span> come here and <span class='line-break'> </span> brought me a hat.<span class='line-break'> </span> [Alma?] had bin to<span class='line-break'> </span> Danville this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning. John come <span class='line-break'> </span> home last night. <span class='line-break'> </span> I want to see him <span class='line-break'> </span> soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2514">
<h3><a name="page-2514">Saturday, September  1, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> finished curing his house<span class='line-break'> </span> of tobacco today. Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> made Franklin two blouses<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. I got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and sewed on some <span class='line-break'> </span> buttons. Today is Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> Smiths birth day. He is <span class='line-break'> </span> eleven years old. <span class='line-break'> </span> They all bathed all the<span class='line-break'> </span> children and put clean <span class='line-break'> </span> clothes on them. <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin went and gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> a big bucket of snaps<span class='line-break'> </span> for me to take with<span class='line-break'> </span> me home tomorrow if<span class='line-break'> </span> I go. That is what I <span class='line-break'> </span> intend. I want to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them all. I have helped<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie the best that I<span class='line-break'> </span> could this week.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope that I may be <span class='line-break'> </span> able to help the <span class='line-break'> </span> rest next week. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2517">
<h3><a name="page-2517">Sunday, September  2, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. I come<span class='line-break'> </span> home today. Marvin and<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and 4 of the<span class='line-break'> </span> children come and<span class='line-break'> </span> brought me. I found <span class='line-break'> </span> them all well and <span class='line-break'> </span> doing well. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> was cureing tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> I will miss Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> so much this week.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope John may <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us<span class='line-break'> </span> and Henry Brumfield <span class='line-break'> </span> two. He is at Johnsons<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> Clifton and his family<span class='line-break'> </span> and Miss Via come <span class='line-break'> </span> to Johnson Reynols<span class='line-break'> </span> last night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that <span class='line-break'> </span> I am at home tonight. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2516">
<h3><a name="page-2516">Monday, September  3, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> fired tobacco all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The others suckered.<span class='line-break'> </span> We folks at the house<span class='line-break'> </span> cooked and churned and<span class='line-break'> </span> [nursed?]. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> the children and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to the tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> patch a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then we went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Bookers. Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> was not at the <span class='line-break'> </span> house. I come home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I come by the pea <span class='line-break'> </span> patch and gathered <span class='line-break'> </span> some peas and shelled<span class='line-break'> </span> them. <span class='line-break'> </span> Clifton Reynols and<span class='line-break'> </span> family and Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield come. <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see <span class='line-break'> </span> them. I have finished<span class='line-break'> </span> stringing snaps for <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner tomorrow.</p>
</div>

<br />
<div id="page-2519">
<h3><a name="page-2519">Tuesday, September  4, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Rain tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> The folks cut tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening. Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Evelyn got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols and spent the<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Clifton and family<span class='line-break'> </span> was there and Miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Georgie Via Jane Reynols<span class='line-break'> </span> aunt. She is a cripple<span class='line-break'> </span> but she is grand.<span class='line-break'> </span> So cheerful and industrious.<span class='line-break'> </span> She sewed nearly all <span class='line-break'> </span> the time I was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Clifton come after me<span class='line-break'> </span> and Christenia brought me<span class='line-break'> </span> home. Clifton carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry home. At least he<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Tim Bennetts<span class='line-break'> </span> on his way home. <span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad to see Miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Via. I had hear about <span class='line-break'> </span> her. Well I wish all<span class='line-break'> </span> of the people well.</p>
</div>

<div id="page-2518">
<h3><a name="page-2518">Wednesday, September  5, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Very hot.<span class='line-break'> </span> They cut tobacco today.<span class='line-break'> </span> John Brumfield come here<span class='line-break'> </span> last night. Reuben Reynols<span class='line-break'> </span> brought him. He went away <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. He started<span class='line-break'> </span> walking. I hope he got a <span class='line-break'> </span> way to ride to Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate harvey come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> us this evening. She<span class='line-break'> </span> brough some snaps. I <span class='line-break'> </span> am glad of them. I<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered some butter <span class='line-break'> </span> beans and Nellie shelled<span class='line-break'> </span> them for dinner tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span> I worked button holes<span class='line-break'> </span> in Franklins blouse.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Nellie milked<span class='line-break'> </span> and Evelyn made bread<span class='line-break'> </span> for supper. I gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> two baskets of tomatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> There is a cloud in <span class='line-break'> </span> the north and I am<span class='line-break'> </span> afraid it will come here. </p>

</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2520">
<h3><a name="page-2520">Thursday, September  6, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day but no rain today.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had the hardest rain<span class='line-break'> </span> and thunder last night<span class='line-break'> </span> that has bin this year.<span class='line-break'> </span> The branch was as high<span class='line-break'> </span> as I ever knowed it to<span class='line-break'> </span> be. The first thing the <span class='line-break'> </span> boys did this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> was to put in the <span class='line-break'> </span> bridge. They moved a <span class='line-break'> </span> curing of tobacco and<span class='line-break'> </span> cut one today. Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker helped them.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr Bookers. This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening I got some <span class='line-break'> </span> snaps. I gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> some peas and shelled<span class='line-break'> </span> them. I gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> the tomatoes today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Want to can them in<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.</p>

<div id="page-2521">
<h3><a name="page-2521">Friday, September  7, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A day that they could [sic]<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the time. They cut<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco. Filled a house <span class='line-break'> </span> and a little on another.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is raining tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie washed some<span class='line-break'> </span> today. I got dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> and churned.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel and I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> barns and to the field<span class='line-break'> </span> where the men was at<span class='line-break'> </span> work. We caught a lot <span class='line-break'> </span> of worms. Looks like they<span class='line-break'> </span> will eat up the tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Bookers hands helped<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The people are so busy<span class='line-break'> </span> that there is not passing<span class='line-break'> </span> a round like [commols to be read common?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey phoned that<span class='line-break'> </span> we could get tomatoes<span class='line-break'> </span> but the boys would<span class='line-break'> </span> not go for them. </p>

Nellie dug some<span class='line-break'> </span> sweet potatoes this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and gathered some peas.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna worked in the <span class='line-break'> </span> field all day of her<span class='line-break'> </span> own chois. No body<span class='line-break'> </span> ask her to. Mabel has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin very good. Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> made some candy.<span class='line-break'> </span> It was very good.<span class='line-break'> </span> Amont them they <span class='line-break'> </span> eat it be for supper<span class='line-break'> </span> and wanted more. <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben will stay <span class='line-break'> </span> at the barns tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry for them.</p>

<div id="page-2533">
<h3><a name="page-2533">Wednesday, September 19, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good dasy. Ben mowed<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Henry staid at the<span class='line-break'> </span> barn. Nellie ironed some. <span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin has not felt well<span class='line-break'> </span> today. I got dinner. <span class='line-break'> </span> Reuban Reynols and<span class='line-break'> </span> Edwin Bumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> come here tonight. Are <span class='line-break'> </span> here now ten oclock. <span class='line-break'> </span> I wrote to Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> today, I am anxious to<span class='line-break'> </span> hear from them. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben Shotwell and Reynols <span class='line-break'> </span> come here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> They wanted to know <span class='line-break'> </span> some a bout how <span class='line-break'> </span> much tobacco they<span class='line-break'> </span> tended this year.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have shell a half<span class='line-break'> </span> gallon of peas for<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.</p>

<div id="page-2535">
<h3><a name="page-2535">Thursday, September 20, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men moved<span class='line-break'> </span> some tobacco this morning. <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben made <span class='line-break'> </span> some boards. Jim went <span class='line-break'> </span> to the saw mill. <span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin went to Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie lost all the milk<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. The bucket handle<span class='line-break'> </span> come out. Edna went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr. Bookers and got <span class='line-break'> </span> milk for the baby. <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to George Blains<span class='line-break'> </span> to the missionary meeting.<span class='line-break'> </span> There wa[sic] several of <span class='line-break'> </span> the neighbors there.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them. I don't belonge<span class='line-break'> </span> with them. Several<span class='line-break'> </span> of them were my<span class='line-break'> </span> grand children.<span class='line-break'> </span> I did enjoy my self<span class='line-break'> </span> fine. Mrs. Edmons brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me home. I was glad.</p>

Johnson Reynols<span class='line-break'> </span> put some in the barn<span class='line-break'> </span> with them. Cardie and <span class='line-break'> </span> Nettie Hendrix and Louise<span class='line-break'> </span> the[y] come and went back<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Nellie and<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner. We cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> turnip salit and corn <span class='line-break'> </span> bread. We did enjoy it. <span class='line-break'> </span> Louise and Herbert and <span class='line-break'> </span> Margaret Hutcherson come<span class='line-break'> </span> and played with the<span class='line-break'> </span> children a while. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Henry has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> hunting tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin is at the [kitchen?]<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. Said she was<span class='line-break'> </span> going to wash [?].<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Mr. Booker's<span class='line-break'> </span> for snaps this evening. </p>

<h3><a name="page-2537">Saturday, September 22, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

The<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco is high in order.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children and I pulled<span class='line-break'> </span> grass from among the <span class='line-break'> </span> turnips.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Evylin <span class='line-break'> </span> and I walked over<span class='line-break'> </span> to Blains. She was as<span class='line-break'> </span> pleasant as could be.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got two pounds<span class='line-break'> </span> of butter. <span class='line-break'> </span> Sallie and Isla and Cordie<span class='line-break'> </span> was at Ernest's to<span class='line-break'> </span> see Lottie.</p>

<p> Fitch come to see his<span class='line-break'> </span> wife and baby last night. <span class='line-break'> </span> He was as wet as he<span class='line-break'> </span> could be when he got here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

Hope they<span class='line-break'> </span> will work it soon <span class='line-break'> </span> before I go home. </p>

<div id="page-2538">
<h3><a name="page-2538">Tuesday, September 25, 1923</a></h3>

Before<span class='line-break'> </span> she commence<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs McLaulin come to<span class='line-break'> </span> spend the day. She had <span class='line-break'> </span> her little boy with <span class='line-break'> </span> her. He is a fine little <span class='line-break'> </span> fellow. I <span class='line-break'> </span> am very glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie has her for<span class='line-break'> </span> a neighbor. She seems<span class='line-break'> </span> to be a fine woman. <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie had snaps and<span class='line-break'> </span> butter beans and<span class='line-break'> </span> sweet potatoes and cake.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have set a round <span class='line-break'> </span> today and rested. <span class='line-break'> </span> Would like to know what<span class='line-break'> </span> they are doing at home. </p>

I hope she may<span class='line-break'> </span> soon get well. <span class='line-break'> </span> We made the trip o.k.<span class='line-break'> </span> I dreaded the road<span class='line-break'> </span> but Reese drove it <span class='line-break'> </span> alright.</p>

Would <span class='line-break'> </span> be glad to know.<span class='line-break'> </span> The teachers had a <span class='line-break'> </span> teachers meeting today<span class='line-break'> </span> so we had the children<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day.</p>

<h3><a name="page-2550">Saturday, October  6, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

I saw Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Mrs McLaut[ghl?]in and<span class='line-break'> </span> several others that I <span class='line-break'> </span> was glad to see.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie has the care of<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylins baby tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin will take the<span class='line-break'> </span> train for Lynchburg in<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning. She will<span class='line-break'> </span> stay at Lenias tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> I washed a little<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Washed the<span class='line-break'> </span> schoolhouse curtains.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna brought them in<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. I brought two <span class='line-break'> </span> pounds of cheese this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2551">
<h3><a name="page-2551">Sunday, October  7, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cool cloudy day. <span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> until late this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car was here at <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner time. Then Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and three little children<span class='line-break'> </span> went with her home and<span class='line-break'> </span> right back. Henry went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone to preaching.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lawson Emerson was here<span class='line-break'> </span> for supper. Henry and <span class='line-break'> </span> Lawson has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> I would like to go <span class='line-break'> </span> some times but I can't.<span class='line-break'> </span> There is no time here<span class='line-break'> </span> to go unless it is<span class='line-break'> </span> some where it suits<span class='line-break'> </span> every one. Evylin is <span class='line-break'> </span> gone and Nellie is<span class='line-break'> </span> having a time with <span class='line-break'> </span> the baby. She must not<span class='line-break'> </span> cry a bit if they<span class='line-break'> </span> can help it.<span class='line-break'> </span>  </p>
</div>

<div id="page-2552">
<h3><a name="page-2552">Tuesday, October  9, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Some frost<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Not enough <span class='line-break'> </span> to kill things. Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco. John<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed. Ben went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the Island for gu[a]no.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Mills worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> road by here. He worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on it all day in sight of <span class='line-break'> </span> the house.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie got a letter from <span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have fixed some rowes <span class='line-break'> </span> in the garden and planted<span class='line-break'> </span> some onions. I could of <span class='line-break'> </span> waited and they would <span class='line-break'> </span> of plowed the land for<span class='line-break'> </span> me but I would not<span class='line-break'> </span> wait. I planted them last<span class='line-break'> </span> year and they made the<span class='line-break'> </span> finest that we every made.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks are tying <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco thnight. Preaching <span class='line-break'> </span> is going on at Strait Stone. </p>

<div id="page-2553">
<h3><a name="page-2553">Monday, October  8, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

They are stripping<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. We sent Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> to tell Jim that dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> was ready. She went and <span class='line-break'> </span> tolde him and then went <span class='line-break'> </span> to John Wards. Her dady<span class='line-break'> </span> switched her a little. <span class='line-break'> </span> Made her very mad.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got Ben to work on <span class='line-break'> </span> the cup board to keep <span class='line-break'> </span> out mice. <span class='line-break'> </span> The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school. <span class='line-break'> </span> I done the cooking.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie has a job<span class='line-break'> </span> attending to <span class='line-break'> </span> Elaine. Mabel says<span class='line-break'> </span> her tooth hurts tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry for<span class='line-break'> </span> her.</p>

<div id="page-2554">

The[y] put<span class='line-break'> </span> some on Mr Bookers waggon<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening to go to <span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school. Nellie kept Elain<span class='line-break'> </span> and helped what she<span class='line-break'> </span> could. She got supper.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to see Lottie<span class='line-break'> </span> Craddock. She has a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> baby. The have not named<span class='line-break'> </span> him yet. Mabel done fine<span class='line-break'> </span> while she was there. She<span class='line-break'> </span> did not like to walk.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr John Tucker ask us<span class='line-break'> </span> to ride on his truck. I<span class='line-break'> </span> was glad of it. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried us nearly there<span class='line-break'> </span> be fore he commenced <span class='line-break'> </span> worke after dinner. <span class='line-break'> </span> I rocked Mabel to sleep<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. <h3><a name="page-2556">Friday, October 12, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear day. Carried us to <span class='line-break'> </span> Danville. We eat dinner at<span class='line-break'> </span> Howard Fergersons. Julia gave<span class='line-break'> </span> us a good dinner. Than we <span class='line-break'> </span> went to the fair grounds.<span class='line-break'> </span> Saw lots of things. Staid<span class='line-break'> </span> unitl after nine o clock.<span class='line-break'> </span> We got a sand witch an<span class='line-break'> </span> a cup of coffee on the grounds.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then we come to Fergersons<span class='line-break'> </span> and eat a snack and come<span class='line-break'> </span> to Johnson Reynols. None of it <span class='line-break'> </span> cost me any thing. Mollie <span class='line-break'> </span> and Posie was good to me.<span class='line-break'> </span> I want to be thankful.</p>

<div id="page-2567">
<h3><a name="page-2567">Tuesday, October 23, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rained and the wind<span class='line-break'> </span> blowed. The folks could<span class='line-break'> </span> not keep warm and <span class='line-break'> </span> strip tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school. If [sic, she may have meant "but"] it was so bad<span class='line-break'> </span> Jo Edmons brought<span class='line-break'> </span> them home on his car.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad as the walking<span class='line-break'> </span> was so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Thomas Brumfield painted<span class='line-break'> </span> one side fo the roof<span class='line-break'> </span> and it nearly all<span class='line-break'> </span> washed off. It will be [tode?]<span class='line-break'> </span> a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have staid in the <span class='line-break'> </span> house nearly all the <span class='line-break'> </span> time. Mrs. Car sent<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel two peticoats.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel was very glad<span class='line-break'> </span> of them. I cut two<span class='line-break'> </span> shirts for Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> today.</p>
</div>

<div id="page-2569">
<h3><a name="page-2569">Wednesday, October 24, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde day for Oct.<span class='line-break'> </span> There will be a freeze<span class='line-break'> </span> by morning I am a <span class='line-break'> </span> fraid. Thomas Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> went from here this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning on the waggon.<span class='line-break'> </span> The school children<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben has stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> some tobacco. They<span class='line-break'> </span> are tying tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> I have cooked enought<span class='line-break'> </span> for them to eat and<span class='line-break'> </span> made Franklin two <span class='line-break'> </span> shirts. I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they are made.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has complained<span class='line-break'> </span> of the tooth ache<span class='line-break'> </span> today. I have finished<span class='line-break'> </span> mending Franklins coat<span class='line-break'> </span> and Edna sweater.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a letter from <span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie today. Was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to her from <span class='line-break'> </span> her and the baby.</p>

<div id="page-2568">
<h3><a name="page-2568">Thursday, October 25, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. Jo Edmons[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> brought Edna and Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> home on his car. Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey is here tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that she<span class='line-break'> </span> come. The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> has worked on their<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day and til<span class='line-break'> </span> bed time tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lelia Ward brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me a piece of beef<span class='line-break'> </span> today. We certainly <span class='line-break'> </span> did enjoy it.<span class='line-break'> </span> I made Mabel an <span class='line-break'> </span> apron today. She has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin as sweet as could [sic]<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the time today. <span class='line-break'> </span> She has a very bad<span class='line-break'> </span> colde.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry brought a rooster <span class='line-break'> </span> from Kates last evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad of him.</p>

<h3><a name="page-2571">Friday, October 26, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> has started to Straight<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone tonight on a car <span class='line-break'> </span> his first trip by <span class='line-break'> </span> him self. I hope that<span class='line-break'> </span> nothing may happen <span class='line-break'> </span> to him.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey went from<span class='line-break'> </span> here this morning. I am<span class='line-break'> </span> so glad that she come<span class='line-break'> </span> to spend the night<span class='line-break'> </span> with us. I picked up<span class='line-break'> </span> all of the walnuts<span class='line-break'> </span> today. The men and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children Edna and Franklin <span class='line-break'> </span> put them in the<span class='line-break'> </span> buggy house up stairs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry come by the <span class='line-break'> </span> store tonight. He got<span class='line-break'> </span> a piece of meat<span class='line-break'> </span> and matches.</p>

<div id="page-2570">
<h3><a name="page-2570">Saturday, October 27, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very good day. Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben worked on tobacco. I <span class='line-break'> </span> got Ben to go to Renan <span class='line-break'> </span> and pay my taxes. That <span class='line-break'> </span> bothered him some but I am<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that it was done.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and John Ward got up <span class='line-break'> </span> the sweet potatoes. We<span class='line-break'> </span> made a good crop. They<span class='line-break'> </span> should of bin got up sooner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sure they won't <span class='line-break'> </span> keep. The children has<span class='line-break'> </span> played out doors most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day. The day has<span class='line-break'> </span> seemed long to me. I <span class='line-break'> </span> have bin busy all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Cooked three meals and <span class='line-break'> </span> churned. Milked twice.<span class='line-break'> </span> Swept the yard some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Shucked a little corn<span class='line-break'> </span> and tied a little tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> I guess I had done a little<span class='line-break'> </span> of so many things [and?]<span class='line-break'> </span> the day seem long.</p>

I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> for them to go. I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to George Blains. I hope that they<span class='line-break'> </span> may get well soon.</p>
