<h3><a name="page-2584">Friday, November  9, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear colde day. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at Dr. Wiggintons<span class='line-break'> </span> last night. He come<span class='line-break'> </span> by the mill and got flour<span class='line-break'> </span> at Johnsons Mill. He got<span class='line-break'> </span> home a bout two oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Jim stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco. I sewed a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> I killed a chicken <span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner. Just at<span class='line-break'> </span> dark to night Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> Power and Lawson and Mildred<span class='line-break'> </span> and Elizabeth and Raymon<span class='line-break'> </span> come. They brought<span class='line-break'> </span> some beef they weighed<span class='line-break'> </span> at Reynolds. The [sic] eat<span class='line-break'> </span> supper here. The little<span class='line-break'> </span> girls stayed all night<span class='line-break'> </span> and will stay a <span class='line-break'> </span> day or two.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2585">
<h3><a name="page-2585">Saturday, November 10, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Renan and got<span class='line-break'> </span> some things that was<span class='line-break'> </span> bought at Kate's sale.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Henry has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr. Mayhews to <span class='line-break'> </span> night. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> here and the Power children<span class='line-break'> </span> have had a good time<span class='line-break'> </span> playing to day. Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> is got the tooth ache<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I cooked a possome<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Some of the folks<span class='line-break'> </span> eat it and some<span class='line-break'> </span> would not.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a letter from<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie today. She said <span class='line-break'> </span> that they were working <span class='line-break'> </span> on the road by there <span class='line-break'> </span> yet.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2587">
<h3><a name="page-2587">Sunday, November 11, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. We all<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home until<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve. Then <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/9118' title='Mr Emerson'>Mr. Emersons</a>. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> come and<span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with us. I <span class='line-break'> </span> was glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am always glad to<span class='line-break'> </span> have any of the <span class='line-break'> </span> children come. Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> and Lizzie went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blains</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> here. Henry carried<span class='line-break'> </span> them on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> can run the car.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> is as cross as<span class='line-break'> </span> can be. I hope she <span class='line-break'> </span> will not get <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2586">
<h3><a name="page-2586">Monday, November 12, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. Rain <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. The men stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day. Would of<span class='line-break'> </span> loaded the wagon if it<span class='line-break'> </span> had bin a good evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mildred Power went<span class='line-break'> </span> with Edna to school. <span class='line-break'> </span> Elizabeth stayed with<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel. I was glad that <span class='line-break'> </span> she did stay. I cooked <span class='line-break'> </span> beef and cabbage for <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Lawson Power<span class='line-break'> </span> come for the children <span class='line-break'> </span> at dark tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> He eat supper with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope they got home<span class='line-break'> </span> ok. We will miss them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope that they my may come<span class='line-break'> </span> a gain when the weather <span class='line-break'> </span> is warm so that<span class='line-break'> </span> Maybel [sic] can go where she<span class='line-break'> </span> pleases. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> here are at the dining<span class='line-break'> </span> room playing rook.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2588">
<h3><a name="page-2588">Tuesday, November 13, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde disagreeable<span class='line-break'> </span> day. The children went <span class='line-break'> </span> to school. Heard yesterday<span class='line-break'> </span> there was a new baby<span class='line-break'> </span> at Clack Hubbands. <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben loaded the<span class='line-break'> </span> wagon with tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> and started to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> today. I hope that they<span class='line-break'> </span> are at Marvin's tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is so lone some<span class='line-break'> </span> here and they both<span class='line-break'> </span> gone. Heard today that<span class='line-break'> </span> Will King was hurt<span class='line-break'> </span> by his truck turning<span class='line-break'> </span> over on him. He was<span class='line-break'> </span> near Gretna. <span class='line-break'> </span> I don't know any thing<span class='line-break'> </span> to write. No one comes<span class='line-break'> </span> to see me and I can't<span class='line-break'> </span> go to see any body. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2589">
<h3><a name="page-2589">Wednesday, November 14, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. Ben and<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim was at Gretna today.<span class='line-break'> </span> They staid at Marvin's<span class='line-break'> </span> last night and eat<span class='line-break'> </span> breakfast there this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> They unloaded their tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> last night. Marvin and <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie was at Mc Laulin[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> until bed time. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel and I eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> by ourselves. Jim come<span class='line-break'> </span> at one oclock. Then I <span class='line-break'> </span> fixed dinner for him. <span class='line-break'> </span> He come with Mr. Booker. <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad when he <span class='line-break'> </span> come. Ben come with <span class='line-break'> </span> the team about sun<span class='line-break'> </span> down. I was very glad<span class='line-break'> </span> when he come. Lelia<span class='line-break'> </span> come and got some <span class='line-break'> </span> salit this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and Jo Edmons<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben has gone hunting.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2590">
<h3><a name="page-2590">Thursday, November 15, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day. John Ward went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the mill with corn <span class='line-break'> </span> the first that has bin <span class='line-break'> </span> carried this fall. I am <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to get some new<span class='line-break'> </span> meal. The squirrel<span class='line-break'> </span> got out of his cage to<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Guess he wont be<span class='line-break'> </span> seen any more a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> here. Ben turned two<span class='line-break'> </span> opposomes loos today and<span class='line-break'> </span> gave John one.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry got a letter<span class='line-break'> </span> from Julia Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Mabel has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> sweet today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lelia washed for<span class='line-break'> </span> us today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wrote two letters<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Did not get <span class='line-break'> </span> any letters today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope we may hear<span class='line-break'> </span> from Nellie tomorrow.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2591">
<h3><a name="page-2591">Friday, November 16, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco all day. <span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school. Henry and Joe<span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Said they were<span class='line-break'> </span> going to pray[?] meeting.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to Renan<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening for <span class='line-break'> </span> coffee. He drove the<span class='line-break'> </span> car. I sent to<span class='line-break'> </span> Denia for butter<span class='line-break'> </span> today. She sent me <span class='line-break'> </span> tow [sic] and a half pounds.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to get<span class='line-break'> </span> it. I stay here and<span class='line-break'> </span> don't see any one<span class='line-break'> </span> and no one to talk <span class='line-break'> </span> to but Mabel. She <span class='line-break'> </span> is as sweet and good<span class='line-break'> </span> as she can be.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2592">
<h3><a name="page-2592">Saturday, November 17, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Saturday. A colde clear<span class='line-break'> </span> day. The men stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day. Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> hauled some wood tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and Joe Edmons went<span class='line-break'> </span> to John Emersons to a <span class='line-break'> </span> social. Ben has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to Johnson Reynols. <span class='line-break'> </span> He had a letter from<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey. She is <span class='line-break'> </span> visiting Virginia Thomson<span class='line-break'> </span> at Welch W. Va. I was <span class='line-break'> </span> surprised to hear that<span class='line-break'> </span> she was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin said I must <span class='line-break'> </span> write that Henry caught<span class='line-break'> </span> a hawk in his steel <span class='line-break'> </span> trap this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children are all<span class='line-break'> </span> bathed and want to go<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvin's tomorrow. <span class='line-break'> </span> I am a fraid the day<span class='line-break'> </span> will be so colde<span class='line-break'> </span> that they cant go.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2593">
<h3><a name="page-2593">Sunday, November 18, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben and the<span class='line-break'> </span> children and I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvin's. Carrie had<span class='line-break'> </span> a good dinner. Fried<span class='line-break'> </span> chicken and tomatoes and<span class='line-break'> </span> macaronie and chees caned<span class='line-break'> </span> peaches and fruit cake. <span class='line-break'> </span> It was all good and nice. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and I and Henry <span class='line-break'> </span> and Reese went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> my sister Nannie Bennett.<span class='line-break'> </span> She has bin sick and<span class='line-break'> </span> looks bad now but<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope she may soon <span class='line-break'> </span> get well. <span class='line-break'> </span> All of Nannies daughters<span class='line-break'> </span> was there. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see them. We come <span class='line-break'> </span> by Tims[or Jims?] and talked<span class='line-break'> </span> with them a minutes.[sic]<span class='line-break'> </span> We got home in good <span class='line-break'> </span> time. I got supper. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Henry has gone some where.<span class='line-break'> </span> To St. Andrews I guess.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2594">
<h3><a name="page-2594">Monday, November 19, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on tobacco all day. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Altavista and <span class='line-break'> </span> carried some tobacco. <span class='line-break'> </span> It solde low. He was not<span class='line-break'> </span> pleased with the sales.<span class='line-break'> </span> Thomas Callans died<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning from a lick<span class='line-break'> </span> that Will Dickerson hit<span class='line-break'> </span> him. I am very sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> that it happened.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening after <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry come home from<span class='line-break'> </span> school all the children <span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone dealing. I could <span class='line-break'> </span> not get any land.<span class='line-break'> </span> Little Avis Emerson is<span class='line-break'> </span> staying with Edna to<span class='line-break'> </span> night. Ben has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mayhews tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> We are bringing all <span class='line-break'> </span> the water from the<span class='line-break'> </span> spring up in the field.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2595">
<h3><a name="page-2595">Tuesday, November 20, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Jim and Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco. Finished<span class='line-break'> </span> a cureing and loaded the<span class='line-break'> </span> car ready to start to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Thomas Callans was<span class='line-break'> </span> buried today. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mr. George <span class='line-break'> </span> Emersons tonight. I think<span class='line-break'> </span> the Emerson girls are fine.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie Gilbert stoped<span class='line-break'> </span> here a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> today. She looks badly. <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope she may get<span class='line-break'> </span> well soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel is bad off with <span class='line-break'> </span> colde. I let her get out<span class='line-break'> </span> two much yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think Mr. Mayhew and<span class='line-break'> </span> the girls has come to <span class='line-break'> </span> play carrums[?]. I guess<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Henry are glad.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2597">
<h3><a name="page-2597">Wednesday, November 21, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. We got up early<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Ben had gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna . I was surprised as I <span class='line-break'> </span> had not heard any thing about<span class='line-break'> </span> his starting up so early. Jim and <span class='line-break'> </span> John stripped tobacco all day. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> come home by eleven oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard today that Bruce <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols wife has a son. <span class='line-break'> </span> The Emerson children has<span class='line-break'> </span> a lot of school children<span class='line-break'> </span> with them tonight. Two <span class='line-break'> </span> of the Worsham children<span class='line-break'> </span> one Milam one Brumfield. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and Jo Edmons<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone down there to<span class='line-break'> </span> night. Jim sent off<span class='line-break'> </span> an ax helve today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I sent some goods<span class='line-break'> </span> to make Edna[she stopped in midsentence]</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2596">
<h3><a name="page-2596">Thursday, November 22, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day. The<span class='line-break'> </span> men stripped tobacco. They are<span class='line-break'> </span> going to load the<span class='line-break'> </span> car tonight. Mabel and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went up to the barn this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. I could not be<span class='line-break'> </span> any help so we come<span class='line-break'> </span> to the house. Had not bin<span class='line-break'> </span> here long when Millie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols come. I was so glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that she come. She brought<span class='line-break'> </span> a few apples. They were<span class='line-break'> </span> very good. The children <span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> and I got a letter from<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie. They were getting <span class='line-break'> </span> on fine from what <span class='line-break'> </span> she said. We had a foot<span class='line-break'> </span> washing here tonight Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin and I. The <span class='line-break'> </span> children has gone to sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel is much<span class='line-break'> </span> better of her cold today <span class='line-break'> </span> and I am so glad.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2599">
<h3><a name="page-2599">Friday, November 23, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> had his car loaded ready<span class='line-break'> </span> to go to Gretna. Did not<span class='line-break'> </span> go until this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> He went and come before<span class='line-break'> </span> sundown. He was pleased<span class='line-break'> </span> with the sales. Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> John stripped tobacco all<span class='line-break'> </span> day. I sewed a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> Cooked three time and <span class='line-break'> </span> washed dishes and churned.<span class='line-break'> </span> I make all sorts of mistakes<span class='line-break'> </span> such as cross the wrong letter.<span class='line-break'> </span> The tobacco that Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> off today was mine and Johns.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was very glad to get<span class='line-break'> </span> my part of the advance.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has bin cross<span class='line-break'> </span> part of the day. She is not<span class='line-break'> </span> well. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. Did <span class='line-break'> </span> not get wet much.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2598">
<h3><a name="page-2598">Saturday, November 24, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner. Then <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and Franklin and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Gretna. We done<span class='line-break'> </span> some shopping. Then <span class='line-break'> </span> went to see Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while. Found <span class='line-break'> </span> them well enough to<span class='line-break'> </span> be about. I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad of that. We got<span class='line-break'> </span> home in good time<span class='line-break'> </span> to get water and<span class='line-break'> </span> wood and get supper.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry drove the car<span class='line-break'> </span> very good I thought.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> he can drive the car.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope that nothing <span class='line-break'> </span> wont happen to <span class='line-break'> </span> make me afraid.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2600">
<h3><a name="page-2600">Sunday, November 25, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. We all<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home except <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry. He went in [camel?].<span class='line-break'> </span> some where we don't know<span class='line-break'> </span> where. Carrie and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> us. I was so glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them. Carrie helped<span class='line-break'> </span> me get dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> She said that Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> was not well. I do hope <span class='line-break'> </span> he may soon be well.<span class='line-break'> </span> They think they have<span class='line-break'> </span> a hard time and they do<span class='line-break'> </span> in some ways but<span class='line-break'> </span> if any thing sould[sic]<span class='line-break'> </span> happen to Marvin serious<span class='line-break'> </span> then they would see a <span class='line-break'> </span> hard time shure[sic].<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben caught a <span class='line-break'> </span> squirel this evening and<span class='line-break'> </span> put him in a cage. <span class='line-break'> </span> Will try to tame him.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2601">
<h3><a name="page-2601">Monday, November 26, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear morning. Cloudy<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and rain<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. Ben went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> with tobacco. Got home a <span class='line-break'> </span> while be fore night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and John stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs. Booker went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Lynch Burg yesterday. <span class='line-break'> </span> Come home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ray Booker come<span class='line-break'> </span> with Franklin home<span class='line-break'> </span> and staid until his<span class='line-break'> </span> mother got home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin up all<span class='line-break'> </span> day but have not<span class='line-break'> </span> felt good all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben got me a <span class='line-break'> </span> pair of shoes today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a card from<span class='line-break'> </span> Hellen Brumfield today<span class='line-break'> </span> wishing me a good <span class='line-break'> </span> Thanks giving day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2603">
<h3><a name="page-2603">Tuesday, November 27, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Cleared<span class='line-break'> </span> up last night. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> has shucked corn all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The tobacco was dry.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had cabbage for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I stewed a pumpkin<span class='line-break'> </span> that Carrie gave me.<span class='line-break'> </span> Think I will make<span class='line-break'> </span> some pies for Thanks<span class='line-break'> </span> Giving dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie made soap<span class='line-break'> </span> here today. I hope it<span class='line-break'> </span> will be good.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am a bout a sleep<span class='line-break'> </span> and git[?] and go to <span class='line-break'> </span> bed.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2602">
<h3><a name="page-2602">Wednesday, November 28, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> school house. They [sic] school<span class='line-break'> </span> broke up at noon. Some <span class='line-break'> </span> of the teachers li[?]ve a good <span class='line-break'> </span> distance. They went home <span class='line-break'> </span> for Thanks giving day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I dressed a hen for our<span class='line-break'> </span> turkey. Carrie gave me a <span class='line-break'> </span> pumpkin. I have cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> it. Guess they will work<span class='line-break'> </span> here. They can be as<span class='line-break'> </span> thankful at work as they<span class='line-break'> </span> could and not work.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Henry has <span class='line-break'> </span> gone to Mr. Mayhew's<span class='line-break'> </span> to play games.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel had a bad cough. <span class='line-break'> </span> I wanted to go to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Hubband this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening but did not get<span class='line-break'> </span> off. Henry come by <span class='line-break'> </span> Renan and got some <span class='line-break'> </span> meat.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2605">
<h3><a name="page-2605">Thursday, November 29, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim worked on his tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. Ben and John Ward <span class='line-break'> </span> and Henry cut and sawed<span class='line-break'> </span> wood this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> John Ward brought two <span class='line-break'> </span> little baskets here this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning. He made them <span class='line-break'> </span> for Carrie Smith. <span class='line-break'> </span> I cooked a hen for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and baked <span class='line-break'> </span> pies. Carrie gave me <span class='line-break'> </span> a small pumpkin, <span class='line-break'> </span> all that I have had <span class='line-break'> </span> this fall. We have <span class='line-break'> </span> got the water to drink<span class='line-break'> </span> from the spring up in <span class='line-break'> </span> the field. The Children<span class='line-break'> </span> hate to bring it so<span class='line-break'> </span> far. I hope that they<span class='line-break'> </span> will dig out the<span class='line-break'> </span> branch soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2604">
<h3><a name="page-2604">Friday, November 30, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day. Clear <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. Ben moved the<span class='line-break'> </span> cureing of tobacco that<span class='line-break'> </span> was packed in the house<span class='line-break'> </span> that John Ward lives <span class='line-break'> </span> in. Put it in the barn<span class='line-break'> </span> ready to strip. They <span class='line-break'> </span> stripped what they<span class='line-break'> </span> could today. Mr. Mayhew <span class='line-break'> </span> and two of the children<span class='line-break'> </span> was here tonight. They<span class='line-break'> </span> played games. Mayhew<span class='line-break'> </span> said he heard that<span class='line-break'> </span> Will Dickerson had<span class='line-break'> </span> bin caught. I hope is<span class='line-break'> </span> the truth. They<span class='line-break'> </span> children has had a <span class='line-break'> </span> good time playing<span class='line-break'> </span> with paper dolls.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin tryed to tie<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim got a letter<span class='line-break'> </span> from his folks. They<span class='line-break'> </span> were well.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2606">
<h3><a name="page-2606">Saturday, December  1, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day. They<span class='line-break'> </span> men stripped tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> except Henry. Ben has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone some where tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope his car did<span class='line-break'> </span> not give him trouble.<span class='line-break'> </span> We think the children<span class='line-break'> </span> has [deletion] chicken pox.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is not hurting<span class='line-break'> </span> them much yet. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> got a letter from<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey today.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is at Welch <span class='line-break'> </span> yet. I would be so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see her.<span class='line-break'> </span> Alma sent the baby<span class='line-break'> </span> dresses by mail<span class='line-break'> </span> today. They fit he[r] nicely<span class='line-break'> </span> and are very pretty.<span class='line-break'> </span> She wore one of them <span class='line-break'> </span> to the barn for her<span class='line-break'> </span> father to see. <span class='line-break'> </span> Well it is eleven<span class='line-break'> </span> oclock . I think I will <span class='line-break'> </span> go to bed. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2607">
<h3><a name="page-2607">Sunday, December  2, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. We all<span class='line-break'> </span> was at home for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then Henry and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Johnson Reynols. They<span class='line-break'> </span> were not at home. Then<span class='line-break'> </span> we went to Clack<span class='line-break'> </span> Hubbands. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to go. I had wanted to<span class='line-break'> </span> go for some time.<span class='line-break'> </span> They seemed to be getting<span class='line-break'> </span> on fine. They have a <span class='line-break'> </span> fine little baby. He <span class='line-break'> </span> is not named yet.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Booker come while <span class='line-break'> </span> I was gone. I would of<span class='line-break'> </span> liked to see her. Think<span class='line-break'> </span> I will go to see her <span class='line-break'> </span> soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry can run the car.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2609">
<h3><a name="page-2609">Monday, December  3, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben and Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> got up this morning at <span class='line-break'> </span> 4 o'clock loaded the<span class='line-break'> </span> car. Henry and Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> loaded Ben's car and<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Booker and Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> loaded Mr. Bookers. They <span class='line-break'> </span> eat breakfast and <span class='line-break'> </span> started to Gretna. They<span class='line-break'> </span> went and unloaded<span class='line-break'> </span> and was back by nine<span class='line-break'> </span> o'clock. Loaded and went<span class='line-break'> </span> back by twelve o'clock.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben got home by ten[?].<span class='line-break'> </span> They are stripping on <span class='line-break'> </span> Jims last cureing.<span class='line-break'> </span> I talked with Effie B. <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. She has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin to Black Burg. She<span class='line-break'> </span> said that Willie B[a?]rns<span class='line-break'> </span> was sick. I am so sorry. <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope se may get <span class='line-break'> </span> well soon. Mabel and [I]<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mr. Bookers.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2608">
<h3><a name="page-2608">Tuesday, December  4, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rain this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They men stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. I was<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry for them coming<span class='line-break'> </span> home through the rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have spent what <span class='line-break'> </span> time I was not cooking <span class='line-break'> </span> or washing dishes<span class='line-break'> </span> mending the children's<span class='line-break'> </span> clothes. Henry and I was <span class='line-break'> </span> going on a trip to <span class='line-break'> </span> see if we could find<span class='line-break'> </span> some body that had<span class='line-break'> </span> butter to sell. The <span class='line-break'> </span> rain prevented.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has bin very <span class='line-break'> </span> good today. Played <span class='line-break'> </span> with her paper dolls.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is a lot of trouble <span class='line-break'> </span> to look after but a <span class='line-break'> </span> sweet childe. I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that she is here.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2611">
<h3><a name="page-2611">Wednesday, December  5, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day. Rained all<span class='line-break'> </span> last night and most of to<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Edna and Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home. Henry went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben stripped tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> They want to kill hogs<span class='line-break'> </span> but can't. The weather is so<span class='line-break'> </span> bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> I killed a chicken for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wrote two letters. <span class='line-break'> </span> Got no litters today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Don't know any thing <span class='line-break'> </span> to write this time.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2610">
<h3><a name="page-2610">Thursday, December  6, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A windy bad day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim finished stripping<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> John Ward went to Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone. Went on the wagon<span class='line-break'> </span> and carried his family.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Booker come and<span class='line-break'> </span> got the scalding<span class='line-break'> </span> tub fixing to kill <span class='line-break'> </span> hogs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry come home to go<span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone but <span class='line-break'> </span> I would not go because <span class='line-break'> </span> it was colde and windy.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has bin very<span class='line-break'> </span> good today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben is not feeling<span class='line-break'> </span> well today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so sorry for him<span class='line-break'> </span> and can't do any thing<span class='line-break'> </span> to help him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2613">
<h3><a name="page-2613">Friday, December  7, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Jim and Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and Norman Booker killed<span class='line-break'> </span> hogs. They killed 7 hogs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lots of others killed today.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is most two warm<span class='line-break'> </span> but I hope that it<span class='line-break'> </span> will keep.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel and I eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> here today by our selves.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks eat at<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Bookers. Mrs. Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> had help and I have none.<span class='line-break'> </span> I took the fat off the<span class='line-break'> </span> entrails by my self.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did not get <span class='line-break'> </span> any mail today except<span class='line-break'> </span> the news.</p>

<div id="page-2612">
<h3><a name="page-2612">Saturday, December  8, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Warm for December.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> cleaning up after hog<span class='line-break'> </span> killing. Lelia ward and <span class='line-break'> </span> I cut up the lard and <span class='line-break'> </span> sausage. I dried up the<span class='line-break'> </span> lard. Ben and Jim ground <span class='line-break'> </span> the sausage. I seasoned <span class='line-break'> </span> it. Ben made little bags<span class='line-break'> </span> and Edna and Ben filled<span class='line-break'> </span> the sacks. Ben washed<span class='line-break'> </span> off the table and washed<span class='line-break'> </span> the dished[?]. Henry and<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> mill at Cedar Forest.<span class='line-break'> </span> Got some corn meal. <span class='line-break'> </span> John Ward washed the <span class='line-break'> </span> chidlins and cleaned<span class='line-break'> </span> the faces and feet and<span class='line-break'> </span> that was a great <span class='line-break'> </span> help. Ben helped<span class='line-break'> </span> me get supper.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad.</p>

<div id="page-2614">
<h3><a name="page-2614">Sunday, December  9, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Found<span class='line-break'> </span> them fixing to come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> us. Carrie gave me a <span class='line-break'> </span> nice cake for Xmas<span class='line-break'> </span> and some butter. I <span class='line-break'> </span> was glad of all that <span class='line-break'> </span> she gave me. She gave<span class='line-break'> </span> us a good dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and the little girls<span class='line-break'> </span> staid here. Ben got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. I think they<span class='line-break'> </span> enjoyed getting their<span class='line-break'> </span> own dinner. <span class='line-break'> </span> We stoped at Mr.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rowland's and got<span class='line-break'> </span> some oil. The got on<span class='line-break'> </span> fine.</p>

<div id="page-2615">
<h3><a name="page-2615">Monday, December 10, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very warm day for<span class='line-break'> </span> December. Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Gretna and got back <span class='line-break'> </span> before light. I did not know<span class='line-break'> </span> that he was gone until he<span class='line-break'> </span> got home. He eat breakfast<span class='line-break'> </span> and loaded and went back.<span class='line-break'> </span> He went to Danville today. <span class='line-break'> </span> He has just come home <span class='line-break'> </span> 8 o'clock at night. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him to Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> He solde his last tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> today. He come home with<span class='line-break'> </span> Ren Worsham and Emmet<span class='line-break'> </span> Craddock. I was glad when<span class='line-break'> </span> he come home. He brought <span class='line-break'> </span> the children some apples<span class='line-break'> </span> and the baby a rubber<span class='line-break'> </span> camel. I fried meat and <span class='line-break'> </span> sausage and caned it. Hope<span class='line-break'> </span> it will keep. Made scraple.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have hardly set <span class='line-break'> </span> down today. Do hope it<span class='line-break'> </span> may get colde by<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2617">
<h3><a name="page-2617">Tuesday, December 11, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

The children went <span class='line-break'> </span> to school. I done all<span class='line-break'> </span> day what I could and<span class='line-break'> </span> noone could tell any thing<span class='line-break'> </span> had bin done.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mollie &amp; [Dessia?] come to<span class='line-break'> </span> see me I was very<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they come it<span class='line-break'> </span> had bin a long time<span class='line-break'> </span> since [Dessia?] had bin to <span class='line-break'> </span> see us. She said she<span class='line-break'> </span> thought that Isla was<span class='line-break'> </span> feeling better than she had<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie said that Bruces<span class='line-break'> </span> wife was in the Hospitle<span class='line-break'> </span> she had a tumor removed<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope she may get<span class='line-break'> </span> well soon<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<div id="page-2616">
<h3><a name="page-2616">Wednesday, December 12, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men cut wood in the<span class='line-break'> </span> woods and Ben hauled.<span class='line-break'> </span> They put some tobacco in<span class='line-break'> </span> the pit. The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school. <span class='line-break'> </span> I got a card announcing<span class='line-break'> </span> the birth of Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> Thomson's baby.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin very busy today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I boiled meat and made<span class='line-break'> </span> scrapple. I brought some<span class='line-break'> </span> water, cleaned out the range,<span class='line-break'> </span> buried my pech<span class='line-break'> </span> seed. I could not get <span class='line-break'> </span> any way to plant <span class='line-break'> </span> them like I wanted to. <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope I may live and <span class='line-break'> </span> plant them. I want them<span class='line-break'> </span> to do some body some<span class='line-break'> </span> good. They were fine<span class='line-break'> </span> peaches. They come from <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin's.</p>

</div>

<div id="page-2619">
<h3><a name="page-2619">Thursday, December 13, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. No rain to<span class='line-break'> </span> stop work. Ben hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> wood all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim graded tobacco. They <span class='line-break'> </span> all worked on tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Gretna to play<span class='line-break'> </span> basket ball. He has<span class='line-break'> </span> not got home yet. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on his chairs<span class='line-break'> </span> last night and is at <span class='line-break'> </span> work on them tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I will be glad when <span class='line-break'> </span> he gets them finished.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel and I have staid<span class='line-break'> </span> in the kitchen most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day. I cooking and<span class='line-break'> </span> washing dishes. <span class='line-break'> </span> She cutting out paper <span class='line-break'> </span> dolls and coloring<span class='line-break'> </span> them with her pencils. <span class='line-break'> </span> Cutting paper is her<span class='line-break'> </span> daily work. Bless her <span class='line-break'> </span> little soul.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2618">
<h3><a name="page-2618">Friday, December 14, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>The ground was<span class='line-break'> </span> covered with snow this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning. The first of <span class='line-break'> </span> real winter we have <span class='line-break'> </span> had. They stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> A load of tobacco passed<span class='line-break'> </span> here this morning through<span class='line-break'> </span> the snow. They seemed to<span class='line-break'> </span> be making it fine.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to <span class='line-break'> </span> school. I think some<span class='line-break'> </span> of them has a colde<span class='line-break'> </span> from going in the <span class='line-break'> </span> snow. Henry got home <span class='line-break'> </span> last night some where<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout midnight. Said <span class='line-break'> </span> he eat supper at Aunt<span class='line-break'> </span> Caries. Said Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> fell and hurt his arms. <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope he may soon<span class='line-break'> </span> be well. Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr. Allen's this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> Will Allen and his wife moved<span class='line-break'> </span> to their selves to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2620">
<h3><a name="page-2620">Saturday, December 15, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear cold day. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> started to Lynchburg to<span class='line-break'> </span> see his wife and daughter.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope he may find them<span class='line-break'> </span> well and doing well. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry drove the car<span class='line-break'> </span> to Gretna. Ben sawed<span class='line-break'> </span> some wood. Mr. Booker <span class='line-break'> </span> helped John Ward and<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry. They got what <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben had hauled.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Booker eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> with us. I cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> hog chidlins. I was a <span class='line-break'> </span> shamed of it as Mr.<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker was here. Hope he<span class='line-break'> </span> did not find it out[?].<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin chilly and<span class='line-break'> </span> sick some this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs. Booker sent me<span class='line-break'> </span> some butter by Ray<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. I was very<span class='line-break'> </span> glad of it. Henry <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to Mr. Mayhew's.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2621">
<h3><a name="page-2621">Sunday, December 16, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben fixed<span class='line-break'> </span> heater in the dineing<span class='line-break'> </span> room. Henry went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Lee Brumfield's a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while tonight. He said<span class='line-break'> </span> he was going to <span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone. Edna and Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> has the chicken pox. <span class='line-break'> </span> The baby has bin cross <span class='line-break'> </span> all day. I have bin<span class='line-break'> </span> most sick all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lelia come and washed<span class='line-break'> </span> dishes this morning. <span class='line-break'> </span> I made out to get<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Mr. Sam Owen<span class='line-break'> </span> come here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Wanted Ben to go and <span class='line-break'> </span> see if he could do any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing for his car. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has not come <span class='line-break'> </span> back yet. Hope he can<span class='line-break'> </span> fix the car so he can<span class='line-break'> </span> run it. We miss Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> very much.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2622">
<h3><a name="page-2622">Monday, December 17, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Gretna with <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco. He staid about<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. We thought Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> would come home with<span class='line-break'> </span> him but he did not. <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope that there has<span class='line-break'> </span> not any thing happened <span class='line-break'> </span> to him. The had has <span class='line-break'> </span> bin a long one to me.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel and I here by<span class='line-break'> </span> our selves. She is broke<span class='line-break'> </span> out with chicken pox.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not rest good <span class='line-break'> </span> last night. I do hope<span class='line-break'> </span> that she may sleep<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. I had a card<span class='line-break'> </span> from  Floyed and a <span class='line-break'> </span> letter from Alma. <span class='line-break'> </span> I am always glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to hear form any of <span class='line-break'> </span> them. Ben had his<span class='line-break'> </span> teeth worked on today.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are giving him trouble<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.</p>
</div>

<div id="page-2624">
<h3><a name="page-2624">Wednesday, December 19, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A fine day. The boys <span class='line-break'> </span> shucked corn the most of <span class='line-break'> </span> they day. Hauled up one<span class='line-break'> </span> load. Oscar Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> com to see Ben a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> sawing their wood. Lee <span class='line-break'> </span> come for the saw.<span class='line-break'> </span> The horses got to the<span class='line-break'> </span> corn pile and eat a <span class='line-break'> </span> lot. I hope it won't <span class='line-break'> </span> hurt them.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school. They had<span class='line-break'> </span> a game played against<span class='line-break'> </span> the Gretna boys. <span class='line-break'> </span> Renan beat.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a new year <span class='line-break'> </span> book today from <span class='line-break'> </span> Lynchburg. Will and Effie<span class='line-break'> </span> sent it. It is very <span class='line-break'> </span> nice. I got a card<span class='line-break'> </span> from Ervin Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> and Mrs. Kent. I am <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to be remembered.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2625">
<h3><a name="page-2625">Thursday, December 20, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><span class='line-break'> </span> A rainy morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks did not<span class='line-break'> </span> do any thing of any account<span class='line-break'> </span> until evening. They picked<span class='line-break'> </span> up some corn and put <span class='line-break'> </span> it in sacks.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school. There is a play<span class='line-break'> </span> over there tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone all but Mabel. <span class='line-break'> </span> She is a bed and a sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna eat supper at<span class='line-break'> </span> John Hutcherson's tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> [E]Ula Mayhew and Gladis<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen was there two.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wrote to Kate Harvey.<span class='line-break'> </span> Wrote part of one to<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie Smith. Nat<span class='line-break'> </span> passed so early that<span class='line-break'> </span> I did not get it in<span class='line-break'> </span> the mail. Jim sent<span class='line-break'> </span> a box of turnip greens <span class='line-break'> </span> to Ruben's today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2626">
<h3><a name="page-2626">Saturday, December 22, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very warm day for <span class='line-break'> </span> Dec. They cut some <span class='line-break'> </span> feed at Booker's and here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not finish. I got dinner. <span class='line-break'> </span> Though[t?] Mr. Booker would<span class='line-break'> </span> be here. He did not stay.<span class='line-break'> </span> After dinner Henry and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Gretna. I <span class='line-break'> </span> bought a pair of shoes<span class='line-break'> </span> and stockens. Come home<span class='line-break'> </span> and put them on. Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> and Jim went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Mt. Airy. Ben bought<span class='line-break'> </span> some paint. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and I come by<span class='line-break'> </span> by Marvin's and got some <span class='line-break'> </span> cakes that Carrie had<span class='line-break'> </span> made for me. <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin's folks was<span class='line-break'> </span> going to a play at<span class='line-break'> </span> the school house. A <span class='line-break'> </span> part of the school <span class='line-break'> </span> building was burned <span class='line-break'> </span> last night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2627">
<h3><a name="page-2627">Friday, December 21, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Very warm <span class='line-break'> </span> for December. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> hauled some stalks and<span class='line-break'> </span> cut some feed for<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Booker.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school for the last time<span class='line-break'> </span> this year. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to Mt. Airy<span class='line-break'> </span> and played ball and <span class='line-break'> </span> got beat. Come home so<span class='line-break'> </span> mad that he cried.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then he went to Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone to meeting at<span class='line-break'> </span> the church. He has not<span class='line-break'> </span> got back yet I don't think.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr. Mayhew and some<span class='line-break'> </span> of the children come<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight to play games.<span class='line-break'> </span> They seam to enjoy<span class='line-break'> </span> them. I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> for them to come. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and his children<span class='line-break'> </span> like to play.</p>
</div>

<div id="page-2628">
<h3><a name="page-2628">Sunday, December 23, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A warm cloudy day. We<span class='line-break'> </span> all staid at home. We<span class='line-break'> </span> had a nice mess of turnip<span class='line-break'> </span> greens and did enjoy them.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Mrs. Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ray come. <span class='line-break'> </span> Alma and Lonnie Bennett<span class='line-break'> </span> come. Alma brough[t]<span class='line-break'> </span> me a fruit cake and<span class='line-break'> </span> a box of candy and<span class='line-break'> </span> two pounds of butter.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so glad of<span class='line-break'> </span> all of the things.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did not have any<span class='line-break'> </span> butter for several<span class='line-break'> </span> days. That is so little <span class='line-break'> </span> that we did not want<span class='line-break'> </span> to eat it. <span class='line-break'> </span> I am so glad to be<span class='line-break'> </span> remembered by the<span class='line-break'> </span> children. Wish I could <span class='line-break'> </span> see them all once <span class='line-break'> </span> more.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2629">
<h3><a name="page-2629">Monday, December 24, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Jim and Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> and Henry went to Renan<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. I boiled a ham<span class='line-break'> </span> and dressed two chickens<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Ben swept<span class='line-break'> </span> the parlor and hall today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a cake and<span class='line-break'> </span> several packages<span class='line-break'> </span> in the mail and <span class='line-break'> </span> the children got<span class='line-break'> </span> several things. I am <span class='line-break'> </span> so glad to be<span class='line-break'> </span> remembered. Every one<span class='line-break'> </span> is so good to me.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim gave me a pitcher.<span class='line-break'> </span> Aluminum. Very nice.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am invited to<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben Easts to dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow. Guess I won't<span class='line-break'> </span> go. Would like to go<span class='line-break'> </span> but some one will <span class='line-break'> </span> have to stay here.</p>

<h3><a name="page-2634">Saturday, December 29, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

There <span class='line-break'> </span> was no one at home<span class='line-break'> </span> so they went home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and the other<span class='line-break'> </span> children went with <span class='line-break'> </span> them to Worsham's. Then<span class='line-break'> </span> we went to Ernest's<span class='line-break'> </span> and staid a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then went to Reynol's.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs. Reynols had not come<span class='line-break'> </span> home from Danville yet<span class='line-break'> </span> so we come home. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben worked on a<span class='line-break'> </span> picture frame all<span class='line-break'> </span> the evening and tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> We certainly did<span class='line-break'> </span> enjoy their visit. Carrie['s]<span class='line-break'> </span> children and Bens can<span class='line-break'> </span> have a good time<span class='line-break'> </span> playing together.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<div id="page-2635">
<h3><a name="page-2635">Sunday, December 30, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy all day. No<span class='line-break'> </span> rain yet. All the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to Mag<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield's and spent<span class='line-break'> </span> the day. Mag had a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Had the first<span class='line-break'> </span> turkey that I seen this<span class='line-break'> </span> Xmas. Ben staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home all day. Mrs. Kellie<span class='line-break'> </span> was at Mag's. 11:30 o'clock<span class='line-break'> </span> Sunday night. Lee and Grace and Elsie<span class='line-break'> </span> East and two children and<span class='line-break'> </span> Hugh Brumfield come and have<span class='line-break'> </span> just gone. I was glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> they come. I enjoyed their<span class='line-break'> </span> company ever so much.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hildah staid with<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna tonight. Henry and<span class='line-break'> </span> Christenia Reynols and Doris<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield and Jamie and<span class='line-break'> </span> Delma Owen went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Ren Worsham's. None of <span class='line-break'> </span> them were at home. </p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2636">
<h3><a name="page-2636">Monday, December 31, 1923</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lightning and thunder<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. We all have<span class='line-break'> </span> bin at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben cut the aspen that<span class='line-break'> </span> I wanted him to. The<span class='line-break'> </span> children carried most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the brush out for<span class='line-break'> </span> me. I washed some <span class='line-break'> </span> few things this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had rain water to<span class='line-break'> </span> use. Hilda is here<span class='line-break'> </span> yet it was so bad<span class='line-break'> </span> she could not go<span class='line-break'> </span> home. They all have<span class='line-break'> </span> tried their [best]. Seven today<span class='line-break'> </span> had to stay in the<span class='line-break'> </span> house most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> time. Henry &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> are at the dineing room<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight studying [puzzles?].<span class='line-break'> </span> The last [entry]for this year.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel says she is glad Hilda<span class='line-break'> </span> did not go home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<h3><a name="page-2637">Memoranda (i)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>I have 11 little chicks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> carried Red to <a href='../subjects/7759' title='Mr Pagget'>Mr</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons Thursday the 14th 1923<span class='line-break'> </span> opened the Last bbl of <span class='line-break'> </span> Flour June the 15th 1922.</p>
